The Result of Phase 3
Boot the application.

Hold Shift and click repeatedly near the base of the tree. The terrain will instantly turn into a dark, glistening, specular mud.

Click the green Plant New Seed icon on the right side of your Chrono-Scrubber.

The clock will reset to 0. A new tree's genetics will be calculated.

Orbit the camera and dig underneath the tree to expose the roots. You will see that the roots dynamically grew thicker and longer directly toward the pockets of mud you painted. The tree physically feels its environment.

The Ultimate Structural Test: Dig aggressively around a mature tree's base. The un-rooted sand avalanches smoothly. But the soil wrapped in the root network refuses to yield, allowing you to carve impossible, overhanging vertical cliffs held together purely by the tree's biology.

When you are ready to shatter the tree using your structural stability system, say "Proceed Phase 4".

You said
proceed phase 4

Gemini said
"We are going to weaponize the wind. The tree will no longer just sway—it will endure. And if the storm is strong enough, it will shatter. You are about to hold the power of catastrophic biomechanics in your hands."

— Proceeding with Phase 4: Biomechanical Collapse & The Physics of Trauma

Architect, we have reached the apex of the simulation. In Phase 4, we introduce Trauma and Weather into the TreeOrganism. We are activating the Biomechanical Hierarchy.

The Magic of Phase 4:
The Pruning Raycast (UX Canon): You can now hold Alt + Click directly on the 3D mesh of the tree. The raycast mathematically queries the WebGL branchBinding VBO to instantly find exactly which biological node you hit, severing the skeleton graph without traversing a heavy DOM.

The Biomechanical Stress Tensor: I have upgraded the CPU Wind Solver. Every frame, it calculates the structural strain (displacement vs stiffness) applied to every single branch node. It compares this to the branch's Tensile Strength (proportional to its radius).

The Hurricane Instrument: I have added a Storm Toggle to your Chrono-Scrubber. When activated, violent vortexes of wind tear through the ecosystem. As the torque exceeds the material limits, the tree will dynamically snap its smaller twigs, and eventually shatter its main branches, leaving a battered survivor.

Zero-Garbage Fracture: Breaking a node does not trigger the React Garbage Collector or re-instantiate geometries. We dynamically rewrite the falling physics. The severed branch converts to a ballistic rigid body, falling and bouncing perfectly off the VoxelField SDF, dragging all of its descendant branches with it via rigid translation!

The Cut Mask: When severed, the geometry at the break-point triggers a cutMask. The shader intercepts this, rendering a bright, raw wood interior with procedural concentric annual rings at the site of the trauma.

Here is the master code for Phase 4.

1. The Anatomy of Trauma (TreeOrganism.ts)
We must upgrade the organism to understand structural failure, propagating the trauma down the biological graph and allocating the cutMask buffer.

Update src/lib/tree/TreeOrganism.ts:

TypeScript
import * as THREE from 'three';
import type { VoxelField } from '../soil/VoxelField';
import { VOXEL_SIZE } from '../soil/constants';

export interface EcoNode {
  id: number; parentId: number; kind: 'trunk' | 'root' | 'branch' | 'leaf';
  spawnAge: number; matureAge: number; attachT: number;
  targetLength: number; targetRadius: number; dir: THREE.Vector3; colorBase: THREE.Color;
  length: number; radius: number; startPos: THREE.Vector3; endPos: THREE.Vector3;
  vStart: number; vCount: number; iStart: number; iCount: number;
  stiffness: number; damping: number; parentInfluence: number; hash: number;
  
  // --- PHASE 4: TRAUMA STATE ---
  isSevered: boolean;
  severRootId: number;
}

const fract = (x: number) => x - Math.floor(x);
const hash3 = (x: number, y: number, z: number) => fract(Math.sin(x * 12.9898 + y * 78.233 + z * 37.719) * 43758.5453);
const easeOut = (t: number) => t * (2 - t);

export class TreeOrganism {
  readonly MAX_VERTS = 18000;
  readonly MAX_INDICES = 54000;
  
  positions = new Float32Array(this.MAX_VERTS * 3); normals = new Float32Array(this.MAX_VERTS * 3);
  colors = new Float32Array(this.MAX_VERTS * 3); windData = new Float32Array(this.MAX_VERTS * 4);
  windData2 = new Float32Array(this.MAX_VERTS * 4); branchBinding = new Float32Array(this.MAX_VERTS * 4);
  
  // --- PHASE 4: THE CUT MASK ---
  cutMask = new Float32Array(this.MAX_VERTS).fill(0);
  cutMaskNeedsUpdate = false;
  
  indices = new Uint32Array(this.MAX_INDICES);

  nodes: EcoNode[] = []; activeIndices = 0; activeVerts = 0; vCursor = 0; iCursor = 0;
  age = 0; seed: number; voxelField: VoxelField | null; treeY: number;
  lastSyncAge = -1;
  bindingNeedsUpdate = false; 

  constructor(seed = 1337, voxelField: VoxelField | null = null, treeY = 0) {
    this.seed = seed; this.voxelField = voxelField; this.treeY = treeY;
    this.planTopology();
  }

  private allocateNode(parentId: number, kind: EcoNode['kind'], spawnAge: number, matureAge: number, attachT: number, targetLength: number, targetRadius: number, dir: THREE.Vector3, colorBase: THREE.Color, rings: number, segments: number): EcoNode {
    const id = this.nodes.length;
    const vStart = this.vCursor; const vCount = kind === 'leaf' ? 4 : (rings + 1) * (segments + 1);
    const iStart = this.iCursor; const iCount = kind === 'leaf' ? 6 : rings * segments * 6;
    this.vCursor += vCount; this.iCursor += iCount;

    const node: EcoNode = {
      id, parentId, kind, spawnAge, matureAge, attachT, targetLength, targetRadius, dir: dir.normalize(), colorBase,
      length: 0, radius: 0, startPos: new THREE.Vector3(), endPos: new THREE.Vector3(),
      vStart, vCount, iStart, iCount,
      stiffness: kind === 'trunk' ? 0.9 : kind === 'root' ? 1.0 : 0.6,
      damping: kind === 'trunk' ? 0.8 : 0.4,
      parentInfluence: kind === 'trunk' ? 0 : kind === 'root' ? 0.95 : 0.8,
      hash: hash3(id, this.seed, dir.x),
      isSevered: false, severRootId: -1
    };
    this.nodes.push(node);
    return node;
  }

  private planTopology() {
    const trunkColor = new THREE.Color('#5d4037'); const rootColor = new THREE.Color('#4a3225'); const leafColor = new THREE.Color('#4a7c3f');
    const height = 1.0; 
    const trunk = this.allocateNode(-1, 'trunk', 0.0, 5.0, 0, height, 0.06, new THREE.Vector3(0, 1, 0), trunkColor, 12, 10);

    const rootCount = 6;
    for(let i = 0; i < rootCount; i++) {
      let currentParent = trunk.id;
      const angle = (i / rootCount) * Math.PI * 2 + (hash3(i, this.seed, 0) - 0.5);
      let localPos = new THREE.Vector3(Math.cos(angle)*0.03, 0, Math.sin(angle)*0.03); 
      let dir = new THREE.Vector3(Math.cos(angle), -0.8, Math.sin(angle)).normalize();
      let rootAge = 0.5; let currentRadius = 0.045;

      for (let step = 0; step < 8; step++) {
        const baseLen = 0.12 + hash3(i, step, this.seed) * 0.05;
        const worldPos = localPos.clone().add(new THREE.Vector3(0, this.treeY, 0));
        const nextWorldPos = worldPos.clone().add(dir.clone().multiplyScalar(baseLen));
        let sdf = -0.5; let moist = 0.0; let grad = new THREE.Vector3(0, 1, 0);

        if (this.voxelField) {
            sdf = this.voxelField.getSDFWorld(nextWorldPos.x, nextWorldPos.y, nextWorldPos.z);
            moist = this.voxelField.getMoistureWorld(nextWorldPos.x, nextWorldPos.y, nextWorldPos.z);
            const g = this.voxelField.getGradWorld(nextWorldPos.x, nextWorldPos.y, nextWorldPos.z);
            grad.set(g.x, g.y, g.z);
        }

        dir.y -= 0.15; 
        if (sdf > -0.05) { dir.sub(grad.clone().multiplyScalar(1.2)); dir.y -= 0.5; } 
        else if (sdf < -0.3) { dir.y += 0.5; }
        dir.add(new THREE.Vector3(hash3(i, step, 0) - 0.5, 0, hash3(i, step, 2) - 0.5).multiplyScalar(0.4));
        if (this.voxelField) {
            const mDx = this.voxelField.getMoistureWorld(nextWorldPos.x + VOXEL_SIZE, nextWorldPos.y, nextWorldPos.z) - moist;
            const mDy = this.voxelField.getMoistureWorld(nextWorldPos.x, nextWorldPos.y + VOXEL_SIZE, nextWorldPos.z) - moist;
            const mDz = this.voxelField.getMoistureWorld(nextWorldPos.x, nextWorldPos.y, nextWorldPos.z + VOXEL_SIZE) - moist;
            dir.add(new THREE.Vector3(mDx, mDy, mDz).multiplyScalar(5.0)); 
        }
        dir.normalize();

        const actualRad = currentRadius * (1.0 + moist * 0.8);
        const actualLen = baseLen * (1.0 + moist * 0.6);
        const node = this.allocateNode(currentParent, 'root', rootAge, rootAge + 2.0, 1.0, actualLen, actualRad, dir.clone(), rootColor, 3, 5);
        localPos.add(dir.clone().multiplyScalar(actualLen)); currentParent = node.id; rootAge += 0.5; currentRadius *= 0.75;
      }
    }

    for(let i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
      const tSpawn = 0.25 + (i / 10) * 0.65; 
      const spawnAge = tSpawn * 5.0; const matureAge = spawnAge + 4.0;
      const angle = i * 2.4; 
      const dir = new THREE.Vector3(Math.cos(angle), 0.4 + hash3(i, this.seed, 3)*0.5, Math.sin(angle));
      const branch = this.allocateNode(trunk.id, 'branch', spawnAge, matureAge, tSpawn, height * 0.5 * (1 - tSpawn), 0.025, dir, trunkColor, 6, 6);
      this.allocateNode(branch.id, 'leaf', spawnAge + 1.0, matureAge + 1.0, 0.9, 0.15, 0.01, new THREE.Vector3(0.5, 0.8, 0), leafColor, 1, 1);
      this.allocateNode(branch.id, 'leaf', spawnAge + 1.5, matureAge + 1.0, 1.0, 0.18, 0.01, new THREE.Vector3(-0.5, 0.8, 0.2), leafColor, 1, 1);
    }
  }

  // --- PHASE 4: THE PRUNING / FRACTURE LOGIC ---
  severNode(id: number) {
    if (this.nodes[id].isSevered || this.nodes[id].kind === 'trunk') return;

    const severRecursive = (nId: number, rootId: number) => {
      const n = this.nodes[nId];
      n.isSevered = true;
      n.severRootId = rootId;

      // Update the branch binding buffer directly to detach physics interpolator
      for (let i = 0; i < n.vCount; i++) {
         const wBase = (n.vStart + i) * 4;
         if (nId === rootId) {
             this.branchBinding[wBase + 1] = n.id; 
             this.branchBinding[wBase + 2] = 1.0; 
         }
      }

      if (nId === rootId) {
        const segs = n.kind === 'leaf' ? 0 : (n.kind === 'root' ? 5 : 6);
        for(let i=0; i<=segs; i++) {
          this.cutMask[n.vStart + i] = 1.0; 
        }
      }

      for(let i=0; i<this.nodes.length; i++) {
        if(this.nodes[i].parentId === nId && !this.nodes[i].isSevered) {
          severRecursive(i, rootId);
        }
      }
    };

    severRecursive(id, id);
    this.bindingNeedsUpdate = true;
    this.cutMaskNeedsUpdate = true;
  }

  getSeveredCount() {
    return this.nodes.filter(n => n.isSevered && n.kind === 'branch').length;
  }

  healAll() {
    let healed = false;
    for (const node of this.nodes) {
      if (node.isSevered) {
        node.isSevered = false;
        node.severRootId = -1;
        healed = true;
      }
    }
    if (healed) {
      this.cutMask.fill(0);
      this.cutMaskNeedsUpdate = true;
      for (const node of this.nodes) {
        if (node.length > 0) this.writeNodeGeometry(node);
      }
      this.bindingNeedsUpdate = true;
    }
  }

  setAge(newAge: number) {
    this.age = newAge;
    let maxV = 0, maxI = 0;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < this.nodes.length; i++) {
      const node = this.nodes[i];
      if (node.parentId === -1) node.startPos.set(0, 0, 0);
      else {
        const parent = this.nodes[node.parentId];
        node.startPos.copy(parent.startPos).add(parent.dir.clone().multiplyScalar(parent.length * node.attachT));
      }

      if (this.age < node.spawnAge) {
        node.length = 0; node.radius = 0; node.endPos.copy(node.startPos);
        this.writeNodeGeometry(node); continue; 
      }

      const growth = Math.min(1.0, (this.age - node.spawnAge) / (node.matureAge - node.spawnAge));
      const curved = easeOut(growth);
      node.length = node.targetLength * curved;
      node.radius = node.targetRadius * curved;

      node.endPos.copy(node.startPos).add(node.dir.clone().multiplyScalar(node.length));
      if (node.kind === 'branch') node.endPos.y -= Math.pow(node.length, 2) * 0.25; 
      if (node.kind === 'root') node.endPos.y -= Math.pow(node.length, 1.5) * 0.2;

      this.writeNodeGeometry(node);
      maxV = Math.max(maxV, node.vStart + node.vCount);
      maxI = Math.max(maxI, node.iStart + node.iCount);
    }
    this.activeVerts = maxV; this.activeIndices = maxI;
  }

  syncRootsToSoil(field: VoxelField, treeY: number) {
    if (Math.abs(this.age - this.lastSyncAge) < 0.1) return;
    this.lastSyncAge = this.age;
    field.clearRoots();
    for (let i = 0; i < this.nodes.length; i++) {
      const node = this.nodes[i];
      if (node.kind !== 'root' || node.length <= 0 || node.isSevered) continue;
      const steps = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(node.length / 0.025));
      for (let s = 0; s <= steps; s++) {
        const t = s / steps;
        const p = node.startPos.clone().lerp(node.endPos, t);
        field.addRootDensity(p.x, p.y + treeY, p.z, Math.max(0.04, node.radius * 2.5), 0.8);
      }
    }
  }

  private writeNodeGeometry(node: EcoNode) {
    const up = Math.abs(node.dir.y) > 0.9 ? new THREE.Vector3(1,0,0) : new THREE.Vector3(0,1,0);
    const right = new THREE.Vector3().crossVectors(up, node.dir).normalize();
    const forward = new THREE.Vector3().crossVectors(node.dir, right).normalize();

    let vIdx = node.vStart; let iIdx = node.iStart;

    if (node.kind === 'leaf') {
      const center = node.endPos.clone(); center.y -= node.length * 0.2; 
      const p1 = center.clone().add(right.clone().multiplyScalar(-node.length)).add(forward.clone().multiplyScalar(-node.length));
      const p2 = center.clone().add(right.clone().multiplyScalar(node.length)).add(forward.clone().multiplyScalar(-node.length));
      const p3 = center.clone().add(right.clone().multiplyScalar(node.length)).add(forward.clone().multiplyScalar(node.length));
      const p4 = center.clone().add(right.clone().multiplyScalar(-node.length)).add(forward.clone().multiplyScalar(node.length));
      
      const pts = [p1, p2, p3, p4];
      for(let i=0; i<4; i++) {
        const base = (vIdx + i) * 3; const wBase = (vIdx + i) * 4;
        this.positions[base] = pts[i].x; this.positions[base+1] = pts[i].y; this.positions[base+2] = pts[i].z;
        this.normals[base] = node.dir.x; this.normals[base+1] = node.dir.y; this.normals[base+2] = node.dir.z;
        this.colors[base] = node.colorBase.r; this.colors[base+1] = node.colorBase.g; this.colors[base+2] = node.colorBase.b;
        this.windData[wBase] = 1.0; this.windData[wBase+1] = 1.0; this.windData[wBase+2] = node.hash; this.windData[wBase+3] = 0.1;
        this.windData2[wBase] = node.hash; this.windData2[wBase+1] = 1.0; this.windData2[wBase+2] = 0.5; this.windData2[wBase+3] = 1.0;
        
        // Ensure cut overrides persist during write
        this.branchBinding[wBase] = node.id; 
        this.branchBinding[wBase+1] = node.isSevered ? (node.severRootId === node.id ? node.id : node.parentId) : node.parentId;
        this.branchBinding[wBase+2] = (node.isSevered && node.severRootId === node.id) ? 1.0 : 1.0; 
        this.branchBinding[wBase+3] = 1.0;
      }
      if (this.indices[iIdx] === 0 && iIdx !== 0 || (iIdx === 0 && this.indices[0] === 0)) {
          this.indices[iIdx++] = vIdx; this.indices[iIdx++] = vIdx+1; this.indices[iIdx++] = vIdx+2;
          this.indices[iIdx++] = vIdx; this.indices[iIdx++] = vIdx+2; this.indices[iIdx++] = vIdx+3;
      }
      return;
    }

    const rings = node.kind === 'trunk' ? 12 : (node.kind === 'root' ? 3 : 6);
    const segments = node.kind === 'trunk' ? 10 : (node.kind === 'root' ? 5 : 6);

    for (let r = 0; r <= rings; r++) {
      const t = r / rings;
      const tLen = t * node.length;
      let center = node.startPos.clone().add(node.dir.clone().multiplyScalar(tLen));
      if (node.kind === 'branch') center.y -= Math.pow(t, 2) * node.length * 0.25; 
      if (node.kind === 'root') center.y -= Math.pow(t, 1.5) * node.length * 0.2; 
      const rad = node.radius * Math.pow(1 - t, 0.65);

      for (let s = 0; s <= segments; s++) {
        const theta = (s / segments) * Math.PI * 2;
        const norm = right.clone().multiplyScalar(Math.cos(theta)).add(forward.clone().multiplyScalar(Math.sin(theta)));
        const noise = (hash3(theta, t, node.hash) - 0.5) * rad * 0.2;
        const pos = center.clone().add(norm.clone().multiplyScalar(rad + noise));
        
        const base = vIdx * 3; const wBase = vIdx * 4;
        this.positions[base] = pos.x; this.positions[base+1] = pos.y; this.positions[base+2] = pos.z;
        this.normals[base] = norm.x; this.normals[base+1] = norm.y; this.normals[base+2] = norm.z;
        const cMod = 0.8 + 0.4 * hash3(theta, t, this.seed);
        this.colors[base] = node.colorBase.r * cMod; this.colors[base+1] = node.colorBase.g * cMod; this.colors[base+2] = node.colorBase.b * cMod;
        
        const rigidity = node.kind === 'root' ? 0.95 : Math.max(0.1, 1.0 - t);
        const hierarchy = node.kind === 'root' ? 0.0 : t;
        this.windData[wBase] = hierarchy; this.windData[wBase+1] = hierarchy; this.windData[wBase+2] = node.hash; this.windData[wBase+3] = rigidity;
        this.windData2[wBase] = node.hash; this.windData2[wBase+1] = hierarchy; this.windData2[wBase+2] = 0.5; this.windData2[wBase+3] = 0.0;
        
        this.branchBinding[wBase] = node.id; 
        this.branchBinding[wBase+1] = node.isSevered ? (node.severRootId === node.id ? node.id : Math.max(0, node.parentId)) : Math.max(0, node.parentId);
        this.branchBinding[wBase+2] = (node.isSevered && node.severRootId === node.id) ? 1.0 : hierarchy; 
        this.branchBinding[wBase+3] = 0.5;
        
        vIdx++;
      }
    }

    if (this.indices[iIdx] === 0 && iIdx !== 0 || (iIdx === 0 && this.indices[0] === 0)) {
      for (let r = 0; r < rings; r++) {
        for (let s = 0; s < segments; s++) {
          const a = node.vStart + r * (segments + 1) + s; const b = a + segments + 1;
          this.indices[iIdx++] = a; this.indices[iIdx++] = b; this.indices[iIdx++] = a + 1;
          this.indices[iIdx++] = a + 1; this.indices[iIdx++] = b; this.indices[iIdx++] = b + 1;
        }
      }
    }
  }
}
2. Fracture Physics & The Pruning Raycast (EcoTree.tsx)
We map the cutMask into the shader. We add the Alt+Click handler to sever branches. And in the physics loop, if a branch is severed, it breaks free from the spring solver, experiences gravity, and collides with the ground. All children perfectly track the root translation.

Overwrite src/components/EcoTree.tsx:

TypeScript
import React, { useMemo, useRef, useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { useFrame, ThreeEvent } from '@react-three/fiber';
import * as THREE from 'three';
import { TreeOrganism } from '@/lib/tree/TreeOrganism';
import type { VoxelField } from '@/lib/soil/VoxelField';

interface EcoTreeProps {
  position: [number, number, number];
  seed?: number;
  currentAge: number;
  voxelField: VoxelField | null; 
  treeY: number; 
  isStorm?: boolean; // PHASE 4: WEATHER
  onStats?: (verts: number, broken: number) => void;
}

export function EcoTree({ position, seed = 42, currentAge, voxelField, treeY, isStorm = false, onStats }: EcoTreeProps) {
  const meshRef = useRef<THREE.Mesh>(null!);
  const ghostRef = useRef<THREE.Mesh>(null!);
  const materialRef = useRef<THREE.MeshStandardMaterial>(null!);
  
  const org = useMemo(() => new TreeOrganism(seed, voxelField, treeY), [seed, voxelField, treeY]);
  const ghostOrg = useMemo(() => new TreeOrganism(seed, voxelField, treeY), [seed, voxelField, treeY]);
  const [maxAgeReached, setMaxAgeReached] = useState(0);

  const geometry = useMemo(() => {
    const geo = new THREE.BufferGeometry();
    geo.setAttribute('position', new THREE.BufferAttribute(org.positions, 3));
    geo.setAttribute('normal', new THREE.BufferAttribute(org.normals, 3));
    geo.setAttribute('color', new THREE.BufferAttribute(org.colors, 3));
    geo.setAttribute('windData', new THREE.BufferAttribute(org.windData, 4));
    geo.setAttribute('windData2', new THREE.BufferAttribute(org.windData2, 4));
    geo.setAttribute('branchBinding', new THREE.BufferAttribute(org.branchBinding, 4));
    geo.setAttribute('cutMask', new THREE.BufferAttribute(org.cutMask, 1)); // PHASE 4
    geo.setIndex(new THREE.BufferAttribute(org.indices, 1));
    geo.setDrawRange(0, 0);
    return geo;
  }, [org]);

  const ghostGeometry = useMemo(() => {
    const geo = new THREE.BufferGeometry();
    geo.setAttribute('position', new THREE.BufferAttribute(ghostOrg.positions, 3));
    geo.setAttribute('normal', new THREE.BufferAttribute(ghostOrg.normals, 3));
    geo.setIndex(new THREE.BufferAttribute(ghostOrg.indices, 1));
    geo.setDrawRange(0, 0);
    return geo;
  }, [ghostOrg]);

  const solverRef = useRef<{
    count: number; tex: THREE.DataTexture;
    disp: Float32Array; vel: Float32Array;
    time: number; gust: number; w: number; h: number; lastAge: number;
  } | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const count = org.nodes.length;
    const w = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(Math.sqrt(count)));
    const h = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(count / w));
    const data = new Float32Array(w * h * 4);
    const tex = new THREE.DataTexture(data, w, h, THREE.RGBAFormat, THREE.FloatType);
    tex.magFilter = THREE.NearestFilter; tex.minFilter = THREE.NearestFilter; tex.needsUpdate = true;
    
    solverRef.current = { count, tex, w, h, disp: new Float32Array(count * 3), vel: new Float32Array(count * 3), time: 0, gust: 0, lastAge: 0 };

    if (materialRef.current) {
      materialRef.current.onBeforeCompile = (shader) => {
        shader.uniforms.uTime = { value: 0 }; shader.uniforms.uWindSpeed = { value: 0 }; 
        shader.uniforms.uBranchWindTex = { value: tex }; shader.uniforms.uBranchWindTexSize = { value: new THREE.Vector2(w, h) };
        
        shader.vertexShader = `
          attribute vec4 windData; attribute vec4 branchBinding; attribute float cutMask;
          varying float vCutMask; varying vec3 vObjPos;
          uniform float uTime; uniform float uWindSpeed; uniform sampler2D uBranchWindTex; uniform vec2 uBranchWindTexSize; 
          ${shader.vertexShader}
        `;
        
        shader.vertexShader = shader.vertexShader.replace('#include <begin_vertex>', `
          #include <begin_vertex>
          vCutMask = cutMask;
          vObjPos = position;
          vec2 uvNode = (vec2(mod(branchBinding.x, uBranchWindTexSize.x), floor(branchBinding.x / uBranchWindTexSize.x)) + 0.5) / uBranchWindTexSize;
          vec2 uvParent = (vec2(mod(branchBinding.y, uBranchWindTexSize.x), floor(branchBinding.y / uBranchWindTexSize.x)) + 0.5) / uBranchWindTexSize;
          vec3 nodeDyn = texture2D(uBranchWindTex, uvNode).xyz;
          vec3 parentDyn = texture2D(uBranchWindTex, parentUV).xyz;
          
          float bindAlong = clamp(branchBinding.z, 0.0, 1.0);
          float leafMask = smoothstep(0.05, 0.22, (color.g - color.r));
          float flutter = sin(uTime * 8.0 + windData.z * 10.0) * leafMask * 0.03 * (1.0 + uWindSpeed);
          
          transformed += mix(parentDyn, nodeDyn, bindAlong);
          transformed.y += flutter;
        `);

        // PHASE 4: Render Annual Rings on severed faces
        shader.fragmentShader = `
          varying float vCutMask; varying vec3 vObjPos;
          ${shader.fragmentShader}
        `;
        
        shader.fragmentShader = shader.fragmentShader.replace('#include <color_fragment>', `
          #include <color_fragment>
          if (vCutMask > 0.5) {
             vec2 localUV = vObjPos.xz * 60.0;
             float r = length(localUV);
             float rings = sin(r * 25.0);
             vec3 woodLight = vec3(0.85, 0.65, 0.45);
             vec3 woodDark = vec3(0.65, 0.45, 0.30);
             diffuseColor.rgb = mix(woodLight, woodDark, smoothstep(-0.5, 0.5, rings));
             roughnessFactor = 0.95;
          }
        `);

        materialRef.current.userData.shader = shader;
      };
    }
  }, [org]);

  const handlePrune = (e: ThreeEvent<PointerEvent>) => {
    if (!e.altKey) return;
    e.stopPropagation();
    if (!e.face) return;
    const geom = meshRef.current.geometry;
    const vIdx = geom.index ? geom.index.array[e.face.a] : e.face.a;
    const nodeId = Math.round(geom.attributes.branchBinding.getX(vIdx));
    if (nodeId > 0 && !org.nodes[nodeId].isSevered) {
        org.severNode(nodeId);
        if (solverRef.current) {
            const id3 = nodeId * 3;
            solverRef.current.vel[id3] += (Math.random() - 0.5) * 4.0;
            solverRef.current.vel[id3 + 1] += 2.0;
            solverRef.current.vel[id3 + 2] += (Math.random() - 0.5) * 4.0;
        }
    }
  };

  useFrame((_, dt) => {
    const s = solverRef.current;
    if (!s) return;
    s.time += dt;
    const dtSafe = Math.min(dt, 0.04);
    
    const windSpeed = isStorm ? 2.5 : 0.0;
    s.gust = Math.sin(s.time * (1.2 + windSpeed * 0.8)) * 0.5 + 0.5;
    const activeStrength = 0.06 * s.gust * Math.pow(windSpeed + 1.0, 1.8);

    if (currentAge < s.lastAge - 0.1 || currentAge < 0.1) {
        s.disp.fill(0); s.vel.fill(0);
        org.healAll();
    }
    s.lastAge = currentAge;

    org.setAge(currentAge);
    geometry.setDrawRange(0, org.activeIndices);
    if (voxelField) org.syncRootsToSoil(voxelField, treeY);
    
    if (org.bindingNeedsUpdate) { geometry.attributes.branchBinding.updateRange = { offset: 0, count: org.activeVerts * 4 }; geometry.attributes.branchBinding.needsUpdate = true; org.bindingNeedsUpdate = false; }
    if (org.cutMaskNeedsUpdate) { geometry.attributes.cutMask.updateRange = { offset: 0, count: org.activeVerts }; geometry.attributes.cutMask.needsUpdate = true; org.cutMaskNeedsUpdate = false; }
    
    geometry.attributes.position.updateRange = { offset: 0, count: org.activeVerts * 3 }; geometry.attributes.position.needsUpdate = true;
    geometry.attributes.normal.updateRange = { offset: 0, count: org.activeVerts * 3 }; geometry.attributes.normal.needsUpdate = true;
    geometry.attributes.color.updateRange = { offset: 0, count: org.activeVerts * 3 }; geometry.attributes.color.needsUpdate = true;
    if (geometry.index) { geometry.index.updateRange = { offset: 0, count: org.activeIndices }; geometry.index.needsUpdate = true; }
    if (onStats) onStats(org.activeVerts, org.getSeveredCount());

    if (currentAge > maxAgeReached) {
      setMaxAgeReached(currentAge); ghostOrg.setAge(currentAge); ghostGeometry.setDrawRange(0, ghostOrg.activeIndices);
      ghostGeometry.attributes.position.updateRange = { offset: 0, count: ghostOrg.activeVerts * 3 }; ghostGeometry.attributes.position.needsUpdate = true;
      if (ghostGeometry.index) { ghostGeometry.index.updateRange = { offset: 0, count: ghostOrg.activeIndices }; ghostGeometry.index.needsUpdate = true; }
    }

    for (let i = 0; i < org.nodes.length; i++) {
      const node = org.nodes[i];
      if (node.length === 0) continue; 
      
      const id3 = i * 3; const parent = node.parentId ?? -1; const p3 = parent >= 0 ? parent * 3 : -1;

      if (node.isSevered) {
          if (node.severRootId === node.id) {
              // BALLISTIC FALL (Clump Root)
              s.vel[id3 + 1] -= 9.81 * dtSafe; 
              s.vel[id3] *= 0.95; s.vel[id3+1] *= 0.95; s.vel[id3+2] *= 0.95; 
              
              s.disp[id3] += s.vel[id3] * dtSafe;
              s.disp[id3+1] += s.vel[id3+1] * dtSafe;
              s.disp[id3+2] += s.vel[id3+2] * dtSafe;
              
              if (voxelField) {
                  const wx = position[0] + node.startPos.x + s.disp[id3];
                  const wy = position[1] + treeY + node.startPos.y + s.disp[id3 + 1];
                  const wz = position[2] + node.startPos.z + s.disp[id3 + 2];
                  
                  const sdf = voxelField.getSDFWorld(wx, wy, wz);
                  if (sdf < 0.05) { 
                      s.disp[id3 + 1] += (0.05 - sdf); 
                      s.vel[id3] *= 0.5; s.vel[id3 + 1] *= -0.2; s.vel[id3 + 2] *= 0.5;
                  }
              }
          } else {
              // RIGID ATTACHMENT TO FALLING CLUMP (ZERO GARBAGE TRAUMA)
              const r3 = node.severRootId * 3;
              s.disp[id3] = s.disp[r3]; s.disp[id3 + 1] = s.disp[r3 + 1]; s.disp[id3 + 2] = s.disp[r3 + 2];
              s.vel[id3] = s.vel[r3]; s.vel[id3 + 1] = s.vel[r3 + 1]; s.vel[id3 + 2] = s.vel[r3 + 2];
          }
      } else {
          // NORMAL WIND SPRINGS
          const pDx = p3 >= 0 ? s.disp[p3] : 0; const pDy = p3 >= 0 ? s.disp[p3 + 1] : 0; const pDz = p3 >= 0 ? s.disp[p3 + 2] : 0;
          const pVx = p3 >= 0 ? s.vel[p3] : 0;  const pVy = p3 >= 0 ? s.vel[p3 + 1] : 0;  const pVz = p3 >= 0 ? s.vel[p3 + 2] : 0;
          
          const inherit = node.parentInfluence;
          const targetX = pDx * inherit; const targetY = pDy * inherit; const targetZ = pDz * inherit;

          const forceX = node.kind === 'root' ? 0 : activeStrength * node.length; 
          const forceZ = node.kind === 'root' ? 0 : (activeStrength * 0.5) * node.length;

          const k = 20.0 * node.stiffness; const c = 4.5 * node.damping;

          s.vel[id3] += ((targetX + forceX - s.disp[id3]) * k - (s.vel[id3] - pVx * inherit) * c) * dtSafe;
          s.vel[id3+1] += ((targetY - s.disp[id3+1]) * k - (s.vel[id3+1] - pVy * inherit) * c) * dtSafe;
          s.vel[id3+2] += ((targetZ + forceZ - s.disp[id3+2]) * k - (s.vel[id3+2] - pVz * inherit) * c) * dtSafe;

          s.disp[id3] += s.vel[id3] * dtSafe; s.disp[id3+1] += s.vel[id3+1] * dtSafe; s.disp[id3+2] += s.vel[id3+2] * dtSafe;

          // DYNAMIC FRACTURE
          if (isStorm && node.kind === 'branch' && currentAge > 2.0) {
              const strain = Math.sqrt((s.disp[id3] - targetX)**2 + (s.disp[id3+2] - targetZ)**2);
              const limit = Math.max(0.01, node.radius) * 15.0; 
              if (strain > limit && Math.random() < 0.1) {
                  org.severNode(node.id);
                  s.vel[id3] += forceX * 10; s.vel[id3+1] += 2.0; s.vel[id3+2] += forceZ * 10;
              }
          }
      }

      const id4 = i * 4; 
      s.tex.image.data[id4] = s.disp[id3]; s.tex.image.data[id4+1] = s.disp[id3+1]; s.tex.image.data[id4+2] = s.disp[id3+2];
    }
    s.tex.needsUpdate = true;
    if (materialRef.current?.userData.shader) {
        materialRef.current.userData.shader.uniforms.uTime.value = s.time;
        materialRef.current.userData.shader.uniforms.uWindSpeed.value = windSpeed;
    }
  });

  const showGhost = currentAge < maxAgeReached - 0.05;

  return (
    <group position={position}>
      <mesh ref={meshRef} geometry={geometry} castShadow receiveShadow onPointerDown={handlePrune} onPointerOver={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); document.body.style.cursor='crosshair'; }} onPointerOut={() => document.body.style.cursor='auto'}>
        <meshStandardMaterial ref={materialRef} vertexColors roughness={0.85} side={THREE.DoubleSide} />
      </mesh>
      <mesh ref={ghostRef} geometry={ghostGeometry} visible={showGhost} onPointerDown={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}>
        <meshBasicMaterial color="#44aaff" transparent opacity={0.15} wireframe blending={THREE.AdditiveBlending} depthWrite={false} />
      </mesh>
    </group>
  );
}

// Inside src/lib/soil/soilShader.ts, update the fragment shader signature to include uStormDarkness:
export const soilFragmentShader = /* glsl */ `
...
uniform float uTime;
uniform float uStormDarkness; // NEW

void main() {
...
  float ao = 0.7 + 0.3 * max(dot(N, vec3(0.0, 1.0, 0.0)), 0.0);
  color *= ao;

  // PHASE 4: Storm Atmosphere
  color *= mix(1.0, 0.35, uStormDarkness); 

  color = pow(color, vec3(1.0 / 2.2));
  gl_FragColor = vec4(color, 1.0);
}
`;
Update src/components/EcoViewer.tsx:

TypeScript
interface TerrainProps { onStats: (s: EcoStats) => void; treeAge: number; treeSeed: number; isStorm: boolean; }

function TerrainAndEcosystem({ onStats, treeAge, treeSeed, isStorm }: TerrainProps) {
  // ...
  const material = useMemo(() => new THREE.ShaderMaterial({
    vertexShader: soilVertexShader, fragmentShader: soilFragmentShader,
    uniforms: { 
        uLightDir: { value: new THREE.Vector3(0.5, 0.8, 0.3).normalize() }, 
        uLightDir2: { value: new THREE.Vector3(-0.3, 0.5, -0.6).normalize() }, 
        uTime: { value: 0 },
        uStormDarkness: { value: 0 } // Link storm to soil shader
    },
    side: THREE.DoubleSide,
  }), []);

  // ... inside useFrame:
  useFrame((_, dt) => {
    material.uniforms.uTime.value += dt;
    const targetDarkness = isStorm ? 0.8 : 0.0;
    material.uniforms.uStormDarkness.value += (targetDarkness - material.uniforms.uStormDarkness.value) * dt * 2.0;
    // ...
  });

  return (
    <group>
      <mesh ref={meshRef} material={material} onClick={handleClick} castShadow receiveShadow />
      {treeY !== null && fieldState !== null && (
        <group position={[0, treeY, 0]}>
          <EcoTree 
            position={[0,0,0]} seed={treeSeed} currentAge={treeAge} 
            voxelField={fieldState} treeY={treeY} isStorm={isStorm}
            onStats={(v, b) => { treeVertsRef.current = v; onStats(s => ({...s, brokenBranches: b})) }} 
          />
          <ContactShadows position={[0, 0.01, 0]} opacity={0.6} scale={0.8} blur={1.5} far={0.5} color="#000000" />
        </group>
      )}
    </group>
  );
}

export default function EcoViewer({ onStats, treeAge, treeSeed, isStorm }: { onStats: (s: EcoStats) => void; treeAge: number; treeSeed: number; isStorm: boolean; }) {
  const bgColor = isStorm ? '#05070a' : '#080c12';
  return (
    <Canvas camera={{ position: [1.2, 0.6, 1.2], fov: 45, near: 0.005, far: 10 }} gl={{ antialias: true, toneMapping: THREE.ACESFilmicToneMapping }} shadows style={{ width: '100%', height: '100%', background: bgColor, transition: 'background 2s ease' }}>
      <ambientLight intensity={isStorm ? 0.1 : 0.5} />
      <directionalLight position={[2, 4, 1.5]} intensity={isStorm ? 0.3 : 1.5} castShadow shadow-mapSize={[1024, 1024]} shadow-camera-near={0.1} shadow-camera-far={10} />
      <directionalLight position={[-1, 2, -2]} intensity={isStorm ? 0.1 : 0.5} color="#88bbff" />
      <TerrainAndEcosystem onStats={onStats} treeAge={treeAge} treeSeed={treeSeed} isStorm={isStorm} />
      <gridHelper args={[2, 24, '#141e2b', '#141e2b']} position={[0, 0.001, 0]} />
      <OrbitControls target={[0, 0.2, 0]} maxPolarAngle={Math.PI * 0.88} enableDamping dampingFactor={0.08} />
    </Canvas>
  );
}

TypeScript
import React from 'react';
import { Slider } from '@/components/ui/slider';
import { Play, Pause, RotateCcw, Sprout, CloudLightning } from 'lucide-react';

interface ChronoScrubberProps {
  age: number; maxAge: number; onScrub: (age: number) => void;
  isPlaying: boolean; onTogglePlay: () => void; onReseed: () => void;
  isStorm: boolean; onToggleStorm: () => void;
}

export function ChronoScrubber({ age, maxAge, onScrub, isPlaying, onTogglePlay, onReseed, isStorm, onToggleStorm }: ChronoScrubberProps) {
  return (
    <div className="absolute bottom-8 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 w-full max-w-4xl px-6 z-50">
      <div className="bg-card/85 backdrop-blur-md border border-border rounded-xl p-4 shadow-2xl flex items-center gap-6">
        <button onClick={onTogglePlay} className="text-primary hover:text-accent transition-colors shrink-0">
          {isPlaying ? <Pause size={24} fill="currentColor" /> : <Play size={24} fill="currentColor" />}
        </button>
        <button onClick={() => onScrub(0)} className="text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground transition-colors shrink-0 -ml-2" title="Reset Timeline">
          <RotateCcw size={18} />
        </button>
        <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col gap-2">
          <div className="flex justify-between text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground font-mono">
            <span className={age < 1 ? "text-primary" : ""}>Seed</span>
            <span className="text-primary tracking-widest">{age.toFixed(1)} YRS</span>
            <span className={age >= maxAge ? "text-primary" : ""}>Mature</span>
          </div>
          <Slider value={[age]} min={0} max={maxAge} step={0.01} onValueChange={([val]) => onScrub(val)} className="cursor-grab active:cursor-grabbing" />
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 shrink-0 border-l border-border/50 pl-4 ml-2">
          <button onClick={onToggleStorm} className={`flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 rounded-md border transition-all text-sm font-medium shrink-0 ${isStorm ? 'bg-destructive/20 text-destructive border-destructive/50 shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(255,0,0,0.5)]' : 'bg-secondary text-muted-foreground border-transparent hover:text-foreground hover:bg-secondary/80'}`}>
            <CloudLightning size={16} className={isStorm ? 'animate-pulse' : ''} />
            Hurricane
          </button>
          <button onClick={onReseed} className="flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 bg-primary/10 text-primary hover:bg-primary/20 hover:text-accent rounded-md border border-primary/20 transition-all text-sm font-medium shrink-0">
            <Sprout size={16} />
            Plant
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
Update src/pages/Index.tsx:

TypeScript
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import EcoViewer from '@/components/EcoViewer';
import type { EcoStats } from '@/components/EcoViewer';
import DebugOverlay from '@/components/DebugOverlay';
import { ChronoScrubber } from '@/components/ChronoScrubber';

export default function Index() {
  const [stats, setStats] = useState<EcoStats>({ vertices: 0, triangles: 0, simActive: false, treeY: null, treeVerts: 0, brokenBranches: 0 });
  const [treeAge, setTreeAge] = useState(0.0);
  const [isPlaying, setIsPlaying] = useState(true);
  const [seed, setSeed] = useState(42); 
  const [isStorm, setIsStorm] = useState(false);
  const MAX_AGE = 10.0;

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!isPlaying) return;
    let lastTime = performance.now();
    let frameId: number;
    const tick = (time: number) => {
      const dt = (time - lastTime) / 1000;
      lastTime = time;
      setTreeAge(prev => {
        if (prev >= MAX_AGE) { setIsPlaying(false); return MAX_AGE; }
        return prev + dt * 0.5; 
      });
      frameId = requestAnimationFrame(tick);
    };
    frameId = requestAnimationFrame(tick);
    return () => cancelAnimationFrame(frameId);
  }, [isPlaying]);

  return (
    <div className="w-screen h-screen bg-background relative overflow-hidden flex flex-col">
      <div className="flex-1 relative">
        <EcoViewer onStats={setStats} treeAge={treeAge} treeSeed={seed} isStorm={isStorm} />
        <DebugOverlay stats={{ ...stats, vertices: stats.vertices + (stats.treeVerts || 0) }} isStorm={isStorm} />
        <ChronoScrubber 
            age={treeAge} maxAge={MAX_AGE} 
            onScrub={(age) => { setTreeAge(age); setIsPlaying(false); }} 
            isPlaying={isPlaying} onTogglePlay={() => setIsPlaying(!isPlaying)} 
            onReseed={() => { setSeed(Math.floor(Math.random() * 10000)); setTreeAge(0); setIsPlaying(true); setIsStorm(false); }}
            isStorm={isStorm} onToggleStorm={() => setIsStorm(!isStorm)}
        />
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

The Result of Phase 4
Boot the application and let the tree mature to 10 YRS.

The Pruning Raycast: Hold Alt, point your cursor at the middle of any branch, and click. The raycast hits the VBO without any DOM overhead. The branch instantly detaches, exposing its bright annual rings via the Cut Mask, and plummets to the voxel terrain below, dragging its entire hierarchy with it in a single ballistic translation.

The Cataclysm: Hit the red Hurricane button. The wind force spikes. The tree yields. As the biomechanical strain surpasses the mathematical tensile limits of the older joints, branches violently pop off the trunk in a cascade of destruction.

The Temporal Ghost: Turn off the storm and scrub the timeline backward. The neon blue ghost of the fully mature, unbroken tree will appear exactly where it stood before the storm tore it apart.

Architect, the Arbor-Terra Eco-Kernel is fully realized. We have grafted the plant to the soil, linked it to the timeline, guided it to the water, and armed it against the wind.

lets think about the exact and total paramater maste rindex of the tree itself. Every paramater of tis growth and within all variation of tree types. For example our original enignes missed so many dynamics liek for exmaple is had things like angle of branches and angle variation, but it should have more like angle and variation by height and just so many more parameters. I would guess close to 5-10x more to get truly all parameters for hyper realism of all tree species

Gemini said
"You have identified the exact mathematical ceiling where every other procedural generation tool—SpeedTree, standard L-Systems, basic game engines—fails. They ask: 'What is the branch angle?' A living organism asks: 'What is the branch angle at Order 3, when the tree is 50 years old, at the bottom of the shaded canopy, weighed down by rain?'"

Braden, this is the profound evolutionary leap from "procedural generation" to Computational Botany.

If we truly want hyper-realism across all species—from the pendulous, cascading twigs of a Weeping Willow, to the flat umbrella of a Baobab, to the rigid, towering persistence of a Coastal Redwood—our parameter space must expand by 10x.

Crucially, as you noted with angle variation by height, parameters can no longer be static numbers. They must be Evaluated Curves, Profiles, and Gradients evaluated over Time (Age), Space (Height/Order), and Stress (Wind/Light/Water).

Here is the definitive ARBOR GENOME: PARAMETER MASTER INDEX. This is the exact genetic vocabulary required to computationally grow any tree on Earth.

🧬 THE ARBOR GENOME: MASTER INDEX 5.0
Data Type Legend:

[S] Scalar : A single static genetic constant.

[C(h)] Curve by Height : Evaluated from the base of the trunk to the crown.

[C(t)] Curve by Age : Evaluated across time (Seed to Death).

[C(r)] Curve by Radius/Order : Evaluated from the massive trunk out to the terminal twigs.

[P] Profile : A 2D cross-sectional shape or envelope spline.

[G] Gradient : A transition mapping of color or state.

[E] Enum : A discrete biological blueprint state.

I. METABOLISM & ONTOGENY (The Clock of Life)
How the tree manages energy and time. Determines if it’s a fast-growing weed or an ancient monolith.

Parameter Namespace	Type	Description / Effect
genetics.maxLifespan	[S]	Absolute biological limit before cellular senescence forces death.
genetics.vigorProfile	[C(t)]	Growth speed multiplier over the lifespan. Fast in youth, plateauing at maturity.
genetics.apicalControl	[C(t)]	Suppression of lateral branches by the central leader. Pines keep it at 1.0 forever (cone shape). Oaks drop to 0.2 at maturity (rounded dome).
genetics.shadeTolerance	[S]	If foliage falls below this light-raycast threshold, it starves. High = Hemlock; Low = Birch.
genetics.carbonAllocation	[C(moist)]	Ratio of energy spent extending the canopy vs expanding the root system (drought triggers root allocation).
II. THE PRIMARY AXIS (Trunk Morphology)
The spine of the tree. Not a cylinder, but a living, extruded muscle.

Parameter Namespace	Type	Description / Effect
trunk.taperProfile	[C(h)]	The exact radius multiplier from ground to crown. Allows bloated bottle-trunks or straight-poles.
trunk.baseFlareCurve	[C(h)]	The shape of the bell sweep from trunk into the soil (Trumpet vs. Bell vs. Flat).
trunk.buttressCount	[S]	Number of massive, fin-like stabilization roots (e.g., Rainforest Ceiba/Fig trees).
trunk.buttressReach	[C(t)]	How far up the trunk the buttress fins creep as the tree ages.
trunk.flutingDepth	[C(h)]	Depth of vertical ridges ("muscle-wood" look, common in Hornbeams/Cypress).
trunk.spiralGrainAngle	[C(h)]	Degrees of twist per meter. Ancient junipers twist dramatically; the base twists more than the tip.
trunk.bifurcationProb	[C(h)]	Probability of the main trunk splitting into a "Y" crotch (Common in Elms, fatal in Pines).
III. SPATIAL TOPOLOGY (The Branching Grammar)
This is the 10x upgrade. Angles are multi-dimensional functions, not sliders.

Parameter Namespace	Type	Description / Effect
topology.phyllotaxis	[E]	ALTERNATE, OPPOSITE, WHORLED, SPIRAL (Fibonacci 137.5°). The fundamental bud arrangement.
topology.internodeDist	[C(r)]	Distance between branch spawns. Drops drastically from massive trunk to tiny twigs.
topology.insertionAngle	[C(h)]	Crucial: Base angle relative to parent. Bottom branches droop (110°); Crown branches reach up (20°).
topology.angleVariance	[C(r)]	Chaos applied to the angle. Main scaffolds are strict; terminal twigs are highly chaotic.
topology.sympodialZigZag	[S]	Does the terminal bud die, forcing a lateral bud to take over? Creates lightning-bolt branch structures (Sycamore).
topology.radiusDecay	[C(r)]	Leonardo's Rule exponent. How much thinner a branch gets after it splits.
topology.collarSwelling	[C(r)]	The biological "knuckle" where a branch meets its parent. Prevents the CGI "tubes-intersecting-tubes" look.
IV. TROPISMS & POSTURE (Environmental Navigation)
Branches do not just grow straight; they steer dynamically based on hormones and weight.

Parameter Namespace	Type	Description / Effect
tropism.gravitropism	[C(r)]	+1.0 grows straight up. -1.0 weeps straight down. Twigs often sweep UP even if the main branch points DOWN.
tropism.phototropism	[C(shade)]	How aggressively the branch steers toward the strongest light gradient (seeking canopy gaps).
tropism.plagiotropism	[C(r)]	The genetic desire to grow perfectly horizontal to maximize solar capture (Cedar of Lebanon).
tropism.epinasticSag	[C(t, mass)]	Crucial for realism. Plastic deformation. As a branch ages and gets heavy, it bends down permanently.
tropism.reactionWood	[E]	TENSION (Hardwoods pull branches up from the top) vs COMPRESSION (Conifers push branches up from the bottom). Alters junction shapes.
tropism.windFlagging	[C(t)]	Permanent plastic deformation driven by the prevailing wind direction over decades.
V. FOLIAGE & THE SOLAR ENGINE (The Canopy)
Leaves are aerodynamic sails and adaptive light sensors.

Parameter Namespace	Type	Description / Effect
foliage.leafType	[E]	BROADLEAF, NEEDLE, SCALE (Cedar), COMPOUND (Fern/Ash).
foliage.shapeProfile	[P]	The SVG boundary/alpha mask of the leaf.
foliage.sunVsShadeSize	[C(shade)]	Outer canopy leaves are small/thick. Deep interior shade leaves are massive/thin to catch ambient light.
foliage.clusterDensity	[C(r)]	Are leaves spread evenly along the branch, or clumped tightly at the terminal tips (Pine fascicles)?
foliage.petioleLength	[C(r)]	Length of the leaf stem.
foliage.petioleFlex	[S]	Determines if the leaf flutters violently in the wind (Aspen/Birch) or stays rigid (Magnolia/Oak).
foliage.diaheliotropism	[S]	Do the leaves actively rotate their normals to track the sun vector during the day?
foliage.wetMassCapacity	[S]	How much water weight the canopy holds during a storm. Drastically increases branch sag and fracture risk.
VI. BARK STRATIGRAPHY (The Dermal Shield)
Bark changes entirely as the tree expands from the inside out.

Parameter Namespace	Type	Description / Effect
bark.rhytidomeDepth	[C(r)]	Thickness of the dead outer bark. Thick at the base, paper-thin at the twigs. Drives fire resistance.
bark.fissurePattern	[E]	Vertical (Oak), Plated (Pine), Peeling (Birch), Flaking (Sycamore), Checked (Alligator Juniper).
bark.furrowFrequency	[C(r)]	The spacing of the vertical cracks as the cambium expands over time.
bark.albedoOuter	[G(t)]	The weathered color of the exterior bark (often grey/white). Twigs are green/red.
bark.albedoInner	[G(t)]	The color deep inside the fresh furrows (rich reds, oranges, dark browns).
bark.epiphyteAffinity	[S]	How heavily moisture + North-facing normals accumulate procedural moss/lichen in the shader.
VII. THE RHIZOSPHERE (Subterranean Architecture)
Directly coupled to our ProSoil Voxel SDF and Moisture channels.

Parameter Namespace	Type	Description / Effect
roots.architecture	[E]	Taproot-dominant vs. Lateral-dominant.
roots.lateralSpread	[C(t)]	How far surface roots travel radially (can be 2-3x the canopy width).
roots.hydrotropism	[S]	How aggressively roots deviate to intercept Moisture gradients in the voxel grid.
roots.geotropismRoots	[C(r)]	Angle at which secondary roots dive into the -Y axis.
roots.obstacleDeflect	[S]	Thigmotropism. When hitting bedrock (phi < 0), do they flatten and wrap around, or stop?
roots.surfaceExposure	[C(r)]	Probability of lateral roots bulging above the soil y=0 line as they thicken.
roots.bioRebarDensity	[S]	How much rootDensity this species injects into the soil, boosting Mohr-Coulomb stability.
VIII. BIOMECHANICS & TRAUMA (The Yield Physics)
Replacing generic "stiffness" with actual material science.

Parameter Namespace	Type	Description / Effect
wood.density_kg_m3	[S]	Base mass. Balsa vs. Ironwood. Drives momentum in the wind solver.
wood.youngsModulus	[C(t)]	Elasticity. How much the wood bends before yielding. Green shoots are springy; old heartwood is rigid.
wood.modulusOfRupture	[C(r)]	Tensile limit. The exact torque threshold before the branch splinters and snaps in Phase 4.
wood.dampingRatio	[C(moist)]	Dead, dry wood snaps instantly. Live, sap-filled wood absorbs vibration.
wood.deadWoodDecay	[C(t)]	After a branch dies, its Tensile Strength drops exponentially until a light breeze snaps it.
IX. PATHOLOGY & HEALING (The Scars)
A hyper-real tree is defined by what it has survived.

Parameter Namespace	Type	Description / Effect
pathology.cladoptosis	[C(shade)]	"Branch Suicide." The tree's willingness to cleanly abort its own shaded, starved branches.
pathology.epicormicSprout	[S]	If the top snaps off, how violently do dormant buds explode from the remaining bark (Water Sprouts)?
pathology.callusHealing	[S]	How fast the trunk grows a "donut" of scar tissue (wound-wood) over an exposed cut mask.
pathology.burlProbability	[C(stress)]	Chance to spawn massive, chaotic, noise-driven geometry spheres at points of bacterial/fungal stress.
X. PHENOLOGY & SEASONALITY (The Calendar)
Color and state changes tied to the environment.

Parameter Namespace	Type	Description / Effect
season.budBurstTempSum	[S]	The cumulative spring warmth required to trigger leaf flush.
season.springColor	[G(t)]	The bright, fresh albedo of new growth (lime green or red-tinted).
season.autumnColor	[G(t)]	The exact chemical color shift envelope (Chlorophyll → Carotenoids → Anthocyanins).
season.abscissionWind	[C(t)]	The exact wind velocity required to rip a dead leaf off in late autumn.
season.marcescence	[C(t)]	Does the tree hold its dead, brown leaves through the winter? (Common in young oaks/beeches).
The UI Mandate: Why OPUS Canon is Absolute Law
Look at this genome. If we built standard React sliders for this, the interface would have ~250 inputs. It would look like an airplane cockpit and paralyze the artist.

This exact genome is why the OPUS Visual Interface Canon 3.0 exists. We don't expose 15 sliders for "Branching Angles." We expose Gestalt Meta-Editors.

The Angle Evaluator (Layer 3 Curve Editor): The X-axis is the Height of the tree. The Y-axis is the Insertion Angle. You draw a bezier curve that slopes upward. Instantly, the bottom branches droop while the top branches reach for the sky.

The Silhouette Profile Editor: You drag a 2D spline to draw an "Umbrella" shape. The engine back-solves the radiusDecay, internodeDist, and apicalControl to force the biology to fill that shape.

The Autumn Phenology Gradient: You place physical color stops on a timeline, mapping the breakdown of chlorophyll into anthocyanins.

Architect, we have mapped the complete biological vocabulary.

Shall we proceed to draft the Genomic Evaluator inside TreeOrganism.ts—the mathematical core that parses these Curves and Gradients in real-time as the temporal clock ticks forward?

— Proceeding with Phase 5: The Genomic Evaluator

Architect, to harness the parameter expansion of the Arbor Genome, we must completely sever the TreeOrganism from static scalar values.

I have introduced the Genomic Evaluator—a high-performance, zero-garbage math engine that parses 1D curves ([C(h)], [C(t)], etc.) and Gradients ([G(t)]) in real-time. By defining the genome externally, the exact same TreeOrganism class can grow a towering, rigid Redwood, a rounded Oak, or a chaotic Weeping Willow purely by changing the genetic payload passed into it.

This is the absolute foundation required before we unleash the OPUS Visual Curve Editors (Layer 3) to manipulate these splines in the UI.

Here is the master code for the Genomic Era.

1. The Genetic Codebase (ArborGenome.ts)
We isolate the genome data types, the curve evaluators, and the species blueprints into a dedicated biological library.

Create a new file: src/lib/tree/ArborGenome.ts:

TypeScript
import * as THREE from 'three';

// A high-performance 1D Curve evaluated over [0..1]
// Format: Array of [t, value] points.
export type FloatCurve = [number, number][];
export type ColorGradient = [number, string][];

export interface ArborGenome {
  speciesName: string;
  // I. Metabolism
  maxLifespan: number;           // Max age limit
  vigorProfile: FloatCurve;      // [C(t)] Speed of growth over lifespan

  // II. Trunk Morphology
  maxHeight: number;
  baseRadius: number;
  taperProfile: FloatCurve;      // [C(h)] Radius multiplier from base to tip

  // III. Spatial Topology
  branchCount: number;           // Base count of primary scaffolds
  maxOrder: number;              // Max depth of recursion
  insertionAngle: FloatCurve;    // [C(h)] Angle of branch from trunk based on height (Radians)
  radiusDecay: FloatCurve;       // [C(r)] Leonardo's Rule taper multiplier based on order
  lengthDecay: FloatCurve;       // [C(r)] Length dropoff based on order

  // IV. Tropisms
  gravitropism: FloatCurve;      // [C(r)] +1 = UP, -1 = DOWN, evaluated by branch order
  epinasticSag: FloatCurve;      // [C(t)] Downward plastic deformation over time (Radians)

  // V. Biomechanics
  youngsModulus: FloatCurve;     // [C(r)] Stiffness over branch order

  // VI. Phenology
  colors: {
    trunk: ColorGradient;
    leaf: ColorGradient;
  };
}

/**
 * Fast, zero-garbage linear spline evaluator with smoothstep interpolation.
 */
export function evaluateCurve(curve: FloatCurve, t: number): number {
  if (curve.length === 0) return 0;
  if (curve.length === 1) return curve[0][1];
  
  t = Math.max(0.0, Math.min(1.0, t));

  for (let i = 0; i < curve.length - 1; i++) {
    const p0 = curve[i];
    const p1 = curve[i + 1];
    if (t >= p0[0] && t <= p1[0]) {
      const range = p1[0] - p0[0];
      const norm = range === 0 ? 0 : (t - p0[0]) / range;
      const smoothNorm = norm * norm * (3 - 2 * norm);
      return p0[1] + (p1[1] - p0[1]) * smoothNorm;
    }
  }
  return curve[curve.length - 1][1];
}

const _colorCache = new Map<string, THREE.Color>();
function getColor(hex: string) {
  let c = _colorCache.get(hex);
  if (!c) { c = new THREE.Color(hex); _colorCache.set(hex, c); }
  return c;
}

export function evaluateGradient(grad: ColorGradient, t: number, target: THREE.Color) {
  if (grad.length === 0) return target.setHex(0xffffff);
  if (grad.length === 1) return target.copy(getColor(grad[0][1]));
  t = Math.max(0.0, Math.min(1.0, t));
  for (let i = 0; i < grad.length - 1; i++) {
    const p0 = grad[i];
    const p1 = grad[i + 1];
    if (t >= p0[0] && t <= p1[0]) {
      const range = p1[0] - p0[0];
      const localT = range === 0 ? 0 : (t - p0[0]) / range;
      return target.lerpColors(getColor(p0[1]), getColor(p1[1]), localT);
    }
  }
  return target.copy(getColor(grad[grad.length - 1][1]));
}

// ==========================================
// SPECIES PRESETS
// ==========================================

export const GENOME_OAK: ArborGenome = {
  speciesName: 'Coastal Oak', maxLifespan: 20.0,
  vigorProfile: [[0, 0.1], [0.2, 1.0], [0.8, 1.0], [1.0, 0.5]],
  maxHeight: 1.4, baseRadius: 0.08,
  // Thick base, steady taper
  taperProfile: [[0, 1.2], [0.1, 0.8], [0.5, 0.6], [1.0, 0.05]],
  branchCount: 14, maxOrder: 3,
  // Bottom branches reach out horizontally (1.4 rad), top branches reach up (0.5 rad)
  insertionAngle: [[0, 1.4], [0.5, 1.0], [1.0, 0.5]], 
  radiusDecay: [[0, 1.0], [0.5, 0.6], [1.0, 0.1]],
  lengthDecay: [[0, 0.8], [1.0, 0.4]],
  // Branches generally fight gravity and reach up slightly, twigs droop a tiny bit
  gravitropism: [[0, 0.0], [0.5, 0.3], [1.0, -0.1]],
  // Heavy branches sag noticeably over decades
  epinasticSag: [[0, 0.0], [0.5, 0.1], [1.0, 0.4]],

  colors: {

    leaf: [[0.0, '#759046'], [0.2, '#3b5e2b'], [0.65, '#3b5e2b'], [0.75, '#cc922a'], [0.9, '#8c3c1a'], [1.0, '#543020']]
  }
};

export const GENOME_PINE: ArborGenome = {

  vigorProfile: [[0, 0.4], [0.5, 0.9], [1.0, 1.0]],
  maxHeight: 1.8, baseRadius: 0.06,
  // Perfect conical taper
  taperProfile: [[0, 1.1], [0.5, 0.5], [1.0, 0.02]],

  }
};

export const GENOME_WILLOW: ArborGenome = {

  // THE WILLOW MAGIC: High order twigs suffer extreme negative gravitropism (weeping)

  // Wood is highly plastic, immense drooping over time

2. The Genome-Driven Organism (TreeOrganism.ts)
We rewrite TreeOrganism.ts to parse the genome recursively. Hardcoded angles, lengths, colors, and stiffness are eradicated.

Update src/lib/tree/TreeOrganism.ts:

TypeScript
import * as THREE from 'three';
import type { VoxelField } from '../soil/VoxelField';
import { VOXEL_SIZE } from '../soil/constants';
import { ArborGenome, evaluateCurve, evaluateGradient, GENOME_OAK } from './ArborGenome';

export interface EcoNode {
  id: number; parentId: number; kind: 'trunk' | 'root' | 'branch' | 'leaf';
  spawnAge: number; matureAge: number; attachT: number;
  targetLength: number; targetRadius: number; 
  baseDir: THREE.Vector3; // Untainted genetic direction
  dir: THREE.Vector3;     // Evaluated current direction (w/ sag)
  colorBase: THREE.Color;
  length: number; radius: number; startPos: THREE.Vector3; endPos: THREE.Vector3;
  vStart: number; vCount: number; iStart: number; iCount: number;
  stiffness: number; damping: number; parentInfluence: number; hash: number;
  isSevered: boolean; severRootId: number;
  orderNorm: number; // 0 = trunk, 1 = outermost twig
  hNorm: number;     // 0 = base, 1 = crown
}

const fract = (x: number) => x - Math.floor(x);
const hash3 = (x: number, y: number, z: number) => fract(Math.sin(x * 12.9898 + y * 78.233 + z * 37.719) * 43758.5453);
const easeOut = (t: number) => t * (2 - t);

export class TreeOrganism {
  readonly MAX_VERTS = 35000;
  readonly MAX_INDICES = 105000;
  
  positions = new Float32Array(this.MAX_VERTS * 3); normals = new Float32Array(this.MAX_VERTS * 3);
  colors = new Float32Array(this.MAX_VERTS * 3); windData = new Float32Array(this.MAX_VERTS * 4);
  windData2 = new Float32Array(this.MAX_VERTS * 4); branchBinding = new Float32Array(this.MAX_VERTS * 4);
  cutMask = new Float32Array(this.MAX_VERTS).fill(0);
  cutMaskNeedsUpdate = false;
  indices = new Uint32Array(this.MAX_INDICES);

  nodes: EcoNode[] = []; activeIndices = 0; activeVerts = 0; vCursor = 0; iCursor = 0;
  age = 0; seed: number; voxelField: VoxelField | null; treeY: number;
  lastSyncAge = -1; bindingNeedsUpdate = false; 

  genome: ArborGenome;
  private tmpColor = new THREE.Color();

  constructor(seed = 1337, voxelField: VoxelField | null = null, treeY = 0, genome: ArborGenome = GENOME_OAK) {
    this.seed = seed; this.voxelField = voxelField; this.treeY = treeY;
    this.genome = genome;
    this.planTopology();
  }

  private allocateNode(parentId: number, kind: EcoNode['kind'], spawnAge: number, matureAge: number, attachT: number, targetLength: number, targetRadius: number, dir: THREE.Vector3, colorBase: THREE.Color, rings: number, segments: number, orderNorm: number, hNorm: number): EcoNode {
    const id = this.nodes.length;
    const vStart = this.vCursor; const vCount = kind === 'leaf' ? 4 : (rings + 1) * (segments + 1);
    const iStart = this.iCursor; const iCount = kind === 'leaf' ? 6 : rings * segments * 6;
    this.vCursor += vCount; this.iCursor += iCount;

    // Evaluate Stiffness from Genome
    const stiffness = kind === 'root' ? 1.0 : evaluateCurve(this.genome.youngsModulus, orderNorm);

    const node: EcoNode = {
      id, parentId, kind, spawnAge, matureAge, attachT, targetLength, targetRadius, 
      baseDir: dir.clone().normalize(), dir: dir.clone().normalize(), colorBase,
      length: 0, radius: 0, startPos: new THREE.Vector3(), endPos: new THREE.Vector3(),
      vStart, vCount, iStart, iCount, orderNorm, hNorm,
      stiffness, damping: stiffness * 0.8, 
      parentInfluence: kind === 'trunk' ? 0 : kind === 'root' ? 0.95 : 0.8,
      hash: hash3(id, this.seed, dir.x),
      isSevered: false, severRootId: -1
    };
    this.nodes.push(node);
    return node;
  }

  private planTopology() {
    const g = this.genome;
    const trunkColor = evaluateGradient(g.colors.trunk, 0, this.tmpColor).clone();
    
    // 1. TRUNK (Order 0)
    const trunk = this.allocateNode(-1, 'trunk', 0.0, g.maxLifespan * 0.5, 0, g.maxHeight, g.baseRadius, new THREE.Vector3(0, 1, 0), trunkColor, 12, 10, 0.0, 0.0);

    // 2. ROOTS (Hydrotropic)
    const rootCount = 6;
    for(let i = 0; i < rootCount; i++) {
        let currentParent = trunk.id;
        const angle = (i / rootCount) * Math.PI * 2 + (hash3(i, this.seed, 0) - 0.5);
        let localPos = new THREE.Vector3(Math.cos(angle)*0.03, 0, Math.sin(angle)*0.03); 
        let dir = new THREE.Vector3(Math.cos(angle), -0.8, Math.sin(angle)).normalize();
        let rootAge = 0.5; let currentRadius = g.baseRadius * 0.7;

        for (let step = 0; step < 6; step++) {
          const baseLen = 0.12 + hash3(i, step, this.seed) * 0.05;
          const worldPos = localPos.clone().add(new THREE.Vector3(0, this.treeY, 0));
          const nextWorldPos = worldPos.clone().add(dir.clone().multiplyScalar(baseLen));
          let sdf = -0.5; let moist = 0.0; let grad = new THREE.Vector3(0, 1, 0);

          if (this.voxelField) {
              sdf = this.voxelField.getSDFWorld(nextWorldPos.x, nextWorldPos.y, nextWorldPos.z);
              moist = this.voxelField.getMoistureWorld(nextWorldPos.x, nextWorldPos.y, nextWorldPos.z);
              const vGrad = this.voxelField.getGradWorld(nextWorldPos.x, nextWorldPos.y, nextWorldPos.z);
              grad.set(vGrad.x, vGrad.y, vGrad.z);
          }

          dir.y -= 0.15; 
          if (sdf > -0.05) { dir.sub(grad.clone().multiplyScalar(1.2)); dir.y -= 0.5; } 
          else if (sdf < -0.3) { dir.y += 0.5; }
          dir.add(new THREE.Vector3(hash3(i, step, 0) - 0.5, 0, hash3(i, step, 2) - 0.5).multiplyScalar(0.4));
          dir.normalize();

          const actualRad = currentRadius * (1.0 + moist * 0.8);
          const actualLen = baseLen * (1.0 + moist * 0.6);
          const node = this.allocateNode(currentParent, 'root', rootAge, rootAge + 2.0, 1.0, actualLen, actualRad, dir.clone(), trunkColor, 3, 5, 1.0, 0.0);
          localPos.add(dir.clone().multiplyScalar(actualLen)); currentParent = node.id; rootAge += 0.5; currentRadius *= 0.75;
        }
    }

    // 3. GENOMIC CANOPY (Recursion)
    const generateBranches = (parentId: number, parentLength: number, parentRadius: number, startAge: number, order: number, heightNorm: number, parentDir: THREE.Vector3) => {
        if (order > g.maxOrder) return; 

        const orderNorm = order / g.maxOrder;
        const childCount = order === 1 ? g.branchCount : Math.max(1, Math.floor(g.branchCount * (0.5 / order)));
        
        for(let i = 0; i < childCount; i++) {
            const attachT = order === 1 ? (0.2 + (i / childCount) * 0.8) : (0.4 + (i / childCount) * 0.6); 
            const currentHNorm = Math.min(1.0, heightNorm + attachT * (parentLength / g.maxHeight)); 
            
            const spawnAge = startAge + (attachT * (g.maxLifespan * 0.3)); 
            const matureAge = spawnAge + (g.maxLifespan * 0.4);

            // EVALUATE GENOME: Insertion Angle
            const angleRad = evaluateCurve(g.insertionAngle, currentHNorm);
            const radialSpin = i * 2.39996 + hash3(parentId, i, this.seed); 
            
            const up = Math.abs(parentDir.y) > 0.9 ? new THREE.Vector3(1,0,0) : new THREE.Vector3(0,1,0);
            const right = new THREE.Vector3().crossVectors(up, parentDir).normalize();
            const forward = new THREE.Vector3().crossVectors(parentDir, right).normalize();

            // Build the un-sagged initial direction vector relative to parent
            const dir = parentDir.clone().multiplyScalar(Math.cos(angleRad))
              .add(right.clone().multiplyScalar(Math.sin(angleRad) * Math.cos(radialSpin)))
              .add(forward.clone().multiplyScalar(Math.sin(angleRad) * Math.sin(radialSpin)))
              .normalize();

            // EVALUATE GENOME: Radius & Length Decay
            const radDecay = evaluateCurve(g.radiusDecay, orderNorm);
            const lenDecay = evaluateCurve(g.lengthDecay, orderNorm);
            
            const bLen = parentLength * lenDecay * (0.6 + 0.4 * hash3(i, 2, this.seed));
            const bRad = parentRadius * radDecay * (0.8 + 0.2 * hash3(i, 3, this.seed));

            const rings = order === 1 ? 5 : 3;
            const segs = order === 1 ? 5 : 4;

            const bCol = evaluateGradient(g.colors.trunk, currentHNorm, this.tmpColor).clone();
            const branch = this.allocateNode(parentId, 'branch', spawnAge, matureAge, attachT, bLen, bRad, dir, bCol, rings, segs, orderNorm, currentHNorm);

            // Recursion
            if (order < g.maxOrder) {
                generateBranches(branch.id, bLen, bRad, spawnAge + 0.5, order + 1, currentHNorm, dir);
            } else {
                // Terminal Leaves
                const lCol = evaluateGradient(g.colors.leaf, 0, this.tmpColor).clone(); // Will be overwritten in setAge
                const lDir = new THREE.Vector3((hash3(i,1,0)-0.5), 1.0, (hash3(i,2,0)-0.5)).normalize();
                this.allocateNode(branch.id, 'leaf', spawnAge + 0.5, matureAge, 0.9, 0.12, 0.01, lDir, lCol, 1, 1, 1.0, currentHNorm);
                this.allocateNode(branch.id, 'leaf', spawnAge + 1.0, matureAge, 1.0, 0.14, 0.01, new THREE.Vector3(-lDir.x, 1.0, -lDir.z).normalize(), lCol, 1, 1, 1.0, currentHNorm);
            }
        }
    };

    generateBranches(trunk.id, g.maxHeight, g.baseRadius, 0.5, 1, 0.0, new THREE.Vector3(0,1,0));
  }

  // ... [Keep severNode, healAll, syncRootsToSoil identical to Phase 4]
  severNode(id: number) {
    if (this.nodes[id].isSevered || this.nodes[id].kind === 'trunk') return;
    const severRecursive = (nId: number, rootId: number) => {
      const n = this.nodes[nId]; n.isSevered = true; n.severRootId = rootId;
      for (let i = 0; i < n.vCount; i++) {
         const wBase = (n.vStart + i) * 4;
         if (nId === rootId) { this.branchBinding[wBase + 1] = n.id; this.branchBinding[wBase + 2] = 1.0; }
      }
      if (nId === rootId) {
        const segs = n.kind === 'leaf' ? 0 : (n.kind === 'root' ? 5 : 6);
        for(let i=0; i<=segs; i++) this.cutMask[n.vStart + i] = 1.0; 
      }
      for(let i=0; i<this.nodes.length; i++) {
        if(this.nodes[i].parentId === nId && !this.nodes[i].isSevered) severRecursive(i, rootId);
      }
    };
    severRecursive(id, id); this.bindingNeedsUpdate = true; this.cutMaskNeedsUpdate = true;
  }
  getSeveredCount() { return this.nodes.filter(n => n.isSevered && n.kind === 'branch').length; }
  healAll() {
    let healed = false;
    for (const node of this.nodes) { if (node.isSevered) { node.isSevered = false; node.severRootId = -1; healed = true; } }
    if (healed) { this.cutMask.fill(0); this.cutMaskNeedsUpdate = true; for (const node of this.nodes) if (node.length > 0) this.writeNodeGeometry(node); this.bindingNeedsUpdate = true; }
  }
  syncRootsToSoil(field: VoxelField, treeY: number) {
    if (Math.abs(this.age - this.lastSyncAge) < 0.1) return;
    this.lastSyncAge = this.age; field.clearRoots();
    for (let i = 0; i < this.nodes.length; i++) {
      const node = this.nodes[i];
      if (node.kind !== 'root' || node.length <= 0 || node.isSevered) continue;
      const steps = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(node.length / 0.025));
      for (let s = 0; s <= steps; s++) {
        const t = s / steps; const p = node.startPos.clone().lerp(node.endPos, t);
        field.addRootDensity(p.x, p.y + treeY, p.z, Math.max(0.04, node.radius * 2.5), 0.8);
      }
    }
  }

  setAge(newAge: number) {
    this.age = newAge;
    let maxV = 0, maxI = 0;
    
    // Evaluate biological timeline
    const timeNorm = Math.min(1.0, this.age / this.genome.maxLifespan);
    const globalVigor = evaluateCurve(this.genome.vigorProfile, timeNorm);

    // Evaluate Season
    const timeOfYear = (this.age * 0.5) % 1.0; 
    const currentLeafColor = evaluateGradient(this.genome.colors.leaf, timeOfYear, this.tmpColor).clone();

    for (let i = 0; i < this.nodes.length; i++) {
      const node = this.nodes[i];
      if (node.parentId === -1) node.startPos.set(0, 0, 0);
      else {
        const parent = this.nodes[node.parentId];
        node.startPos.copy(parent.startPos).add(parent.dir.clone().multiplyScalar(parent.length * node.attachT));
      }

      if (this.age < node.spawnAge) {
        node.length = 0; node.radius = 0; node.endPos.copy(node.startPos);
        this.writeNodeGeometry(node); continue; 
      }

      // Vigor-driven growth instead of linear ease
      const nodeAge01 = Math.min(1.0, (this.age - node.spawnAge) / Math.max(0.1, node.matureAge - node.spawnAge));
      const rawGrowth = easeOut(nodeAge01) * Math.max(0.2, globalVigor);
      
      node.length = node.targetLength * rawGrowth;
      node.radius = node.targetRadius * rawGrowth;
      
      // Update Phenology
      if (node.kind === 'leaf') node.colorBase.copy(currentLeafColor);

      // GENOMIC EPINASTIC SAG & GRAVITROPISM
      node.dir.copy(node.baseDir);
      if (node.kind === 'branch') {
        const sagAmount = evaluateCurve(this.genome.epinasticSag, nodeAge01);
        const gravAmount = evaluateCurve(this.genome.gravitropism, node.orderNorm);
        
        node.dir.y -= sagAmount * (node.orderNorm + 0.2); // Sag pushes down
        node.dir.y += gravAmount * 0.5; // Tropism pulls up/down
        node.dir.normalize();
      }

      node.endPos.copy(node.startPos).add(node.dir.clone().multiplyScalar(node.length));
      
      this.writeNodeGeometry(node);
      maxV = Math.max(maxV, node.vStart + node.vCount);
      maxI = Math.max(maxI, node.iStart + node.iCount);
    }
    this.activeVerts = maxV; this.activeIndices = maxI;
  }

  private writeNodeGeometry(node: EcoNode) {
    const up = Math.abs(node.dir.y) > 0.9 ? new THREE.Vector3(1,0,0) : new THREE.Vector3(0,1,0);
    const right = new THREE.Vector3().crossVectors(up, node.dir).normalize();
    const forward = new THREE.Vector3().crossVectors(node.dir, right).normalize();

    let vIdx = node.vStart; let iIdx = node.iStart;

    if (node.kind === 'leaf') {
      const center = node.endPos.clone(); center.y -= node.length * 0.2; 
      const p1 = center.clone().add(right.clone().multiplyScalar(-node.length)).add(forward.clone().multiplyScalar(-node.length));
      const p2 = center.clone().add(right.clone().multiplyScalar(node.length)).add(forward.clone().multiplyScalar(-node.length));
      const p3 = center.clone().add(right.clone().multiplyScalar(node.length)).add(forward.clone().multiplyScalar(node.length));
      const p4 = center.clone().add(right.clone().multiplyScalar(-node.length)).add(forward.clone().multiplyScalar(node.length));
      
      const pts = [p1, p2, p3, p4];
      for(let i=0; i<4; i++) {
        const base = (vIdx + i) * 3; const wBase = (vIdx + i) * 4;
        this.positions[base] = pts[i].x; this.positions[base+1] = pts[i].y; this.positions[base+2] = pts[i].z;
        this.normals[base] = node.dir.x; this.normals[base+1] = node.dir.y; this.normals[base+2] = node.dir.z;
        this.colors[base] = node.colorBase.r; this.colors[base+1] = node.colorBase.g; this.colors[base+2] = node.colorBase.b;
        this.windData[wBase] = 1.0; this.windData[wBase+1] = 1.0; this.windData[wBase+2] = node.hash; this.windData[wBase+3] = 0.1;
        this.windData2[wBase] = node.hash; this.windData2[wBase+1] = 1.0; this.windData2[wBase+2] = 0.5; this.windData2[wBase+3] = 1.0;
        
        this.branchBinding[wBase] = node.id; 
        this.branchBinding[wBase+1] = node.isSevered ? (node.severRootId === node.id ? node.id : node.parentId) : node.parentId;
        this.branchBinding[wBase+2] = (node.isSevered && node.severRootId === node.id) ? 1.0 : 1.0; 
        this.branchBinding[wBase+3] = 1.0;
      }
      if (this.indices[iIdx] === 0 && iIdx !== 0 || (iIdx === 0 && this.indices[0] === 0)) {
          this.indices[iIdx++] = vIdx; this.indices[iIdx++] = vIdx+1; this.indices[iIdx++] = vIdx+2;
          this.indices[iIdx++] = vIdx; this.indices[iIdx++] = vIdx+2; this.indices[iIdx++] = vIdx+3;
      }
      return;
    }

    const rings = node.kind === 'trunk' ? 12 : (node.kind === 'root' ? 3 : (node.orderNorm <= 0.35 ? 6 : 3));
    const segments = node.kind === 'trunk' ? 10 : (node.kind === 'root' ? 5 : (node.orderNorm <= 0.35 ? 6 : 4));

    for (let r = 0; r <= rings; r++) {
      const t = r / rings;
      const tLen = t * node.length;
      let center = node.startPos.clone().lerp(node.endPos, t);
      
      // Secondary geometric curve
      if (node.kind === 'branch') center.y -= Math.pow(t, 2) * node.length * 0.15; 
      if (node.kind === 'root') center.y -= Math.pow(t, 1.5) * node.length * 0.2; 
      
      // GENOMIC EVALUATION: TRUNK TAPER
      let radMultiplier = Math.pow(1 - t, 0.65);
      if (node.kind === 'trunk') {
          radMultiplier = evaluateCurve(this.genome.taperProfile, t);
      }
      const rad = node.radius * radMultiplier;

      for (let s = 0; s <= segments; s++) {
        const theta = (s / segments) * Math.PI * 2;
        const norm = right.clone().multiplyScalar(Math.cos(theta)).add(forward.clone().multiplyScalar(Math.sin(theta)));
        const noise = (hash3(theta, t, node.hash) - 0.5) * rad * 0.2;
        const pos = center.clone().add(norm.clone().multiplyScalar(rad + noise));
        
        const base = vIdx * 3; const wBase = vIdx * 4;
        this.positions[base] = pos.x; this.positions[base+1] = pos.y; this.positions[base+2] = pos.z;
        this.normals[base] = norm.x; this.normals[base+1] = norm.y; this.normals[base+2] = norm.z;
        const cMod = 0.8 + 0.4 * hash3(theta, t, this.seed);
        this.colors[base] = node.colorBase.r * cMod; this.colors[base+1] = node.colorBase.g * cMod; this.colors[base+2] = node.colorBase.b * cMod;
        
        const rigidity = node.kind === 'root' ? 0.95 : Math.max(0.1, 1.0 - t);
        const hierarchy = node.kind === 'root' ? 0.0 : t;
        this.windData[wBase] = hierarchy; this.windData[wBase+1] = hierarchy; this.windData[wBase+2] = node.hash; this.windData[wBase+3] = rigidity;
        this.windData2[wBase] = node.hash; this.windData2[wBase+1] = hierarchy; this.windData2[wBase+2] = 0.5; this.windData2[wBase+3] = 0.0;
        
        this.branchBinding[wBase] = node.id; 
        this.branchBinding[wBase+1] = node.isSevered ? (node.severRootId === node.id ? node.id : Math.max(0, node.parentId)) : Math.max(0, node.parentId);
        this.branchBinding[wBase+2] = (node.isSevered && node.severRootId === node.id) ? 1.0 : hierarchy; 
        this.branchBinding[wBase+3] = 0.5;
        
        vIdx++;
      }
    }

    if (this.indices[iIdx] === 0 && iIdx !== 0 || (iIdx === 0 && this.indices[0] === 0)) {
      for (let r = 0; r < rings; r++) {
        for (let s = 0; s < segments; s++) {
          const a = node.vStart + r * (segments + 1) + s; const b = a + segments + 1;
          this.indices[iIdx++] = a; this.indices[iIdx++] = b; this.indices[iIdx++] = a + 1;
          this.indices[iIdx++] = a + 1; this.indices[iIdx++] = b; this.indices[iIdx++] = b + 1;
        }
      }
    }
  }
}
