2. Budding & Volumetric Leaf Clusters (TreeOrganism.ts)
We upgrade the Organism to support Volumetric Leaves (8 vertices, intersecting planes) and track the biological leafScale through the seasons.

Update src/lib/tree/TreeOrganism.ts:

TypeScript
import * as THREE from 'three';
import type { VoxelField } from '../soil/VoxelField';
import { VOXEL_SIZE } from '../soil/constants';
import { ArborGenome, evaluateCurve, evaluateGradient, GENOME_OAK } from './ArborGenome';

export interface EcoNode {
  id: number; parentId: number; kind: 'trunk' | 'root' | 'branch' | 'leaf';
  spawnAge: number; matureAge: number; attachT: number;
  targetLength: number; targetRadius: number; 
  baseDir: THREE.Vector3; dir: THREE.Vector3; colorBase: THREE.Color;
  length: number; radius: number; startPos: THREE.Vector3; endPos: THREE.Vector3;
  vStart: number; vCount: number; iStart: number; iCount: number;
  stiffness: number; damping: number; parentInfluence: number; hash: number;
  isSevered: boolean; severRootId: number;
  orderNorm: number; hNorm: number;
  
  // --- PHASE 7: FOLIAGE TRACKING ---
  cycleOffset: number;
  leafScale: number; 
  isSettled: boolean;
  justHealed: boolean;
}

const fract = (x: number) => x - Math.floor(x);
const hash3 = (x: number, y: number, z: number) => fract(Math.sin(x * 12.9898 + y * 78.233 + z * 37.719) * 43758.5453);
const easeOut = (t: number) => t * (2 - t);

export class TreeOrganism {
  readonly MAX_VERTS = 65000;
  readonly MAX_INDICES = 195000;
  
  positions = new Float32Array(this.MAX_VERTS * 3); normals = new Float32Array(this.MAX_VERTS * 3);
  colors = new Float32Array(this.MAX_VERTS * 3); windData = new Float32Array(this.MAX_VERTS * 4);
  windData2 = new Float32Array(this.MAX_VERTS * 4); branchBinding = new Float32Array(this.MAX_VERTS * 4);
  cutMask = new Float32Array(this.MAX_VERTS).fill(0);
  indices = new Uint32Array(this.MAX_INDICES);

  nodes: EcoNode[] = []; nodeCount = 0; 
  activeIndices = 0; activeVerts = 0; vCursor = 0; iCursor = 0;
  age = 0; seed: number; voxelField: VoxelField | null; treeY: number;
  lastSyncAge = -1; bindingNeedsUpdate = false; cutMaskNeedsUpdate = false;

  genome: ArborGenome;
  private tmpColor = new THREE.Color();

  constructor(seed = 1337, voxelField: VoxelField | null = null, treeY = 0, genome: ArborGenome = GENOME_OAK) {
    this.seed = seed; this.voxelField = voxelField; this.treeY = treeY;
    this.genome = genome;
    this.planTopology();
  }

  updateGenome(newGenome: ArborGenome) { this.genome = newGenome; this.rebuildTopology(); }

  rebuildTopology() {
    this.nodeCount = 0; this.vCursor = 0; this.iCursor = 0; this.activeVerts = 0; this.activeIndices = 0;
    this.indices.fill(0); 
    this.planTopology(); this.setAge(this.age, false); 
    this.bindingNeedsUpdate = true; this.cutMaskNeedsUpdate = true;
  }

  private allocateNode(parentId: number, kind: EcoNode['kind'], spawnAge: number, matureAge: number, attachT: number, targetLength: number, targetRadius: number, dir: THREE.Vector3, colorBase: THREE.Color, rings: number, segments: number, orderNorm: number, hNorm: number): EcoNode {
    const id = this.nodeCount;
    // PHASE 7: LEAVES ARE NOW VOLUMETRIC (8 Verts, 12 Indices)
    const vStart = this.vCursor; const vCount = kind === 'leaf' ? 8 : (rings + 1) * (segments + 1);
    const iStart = this.iCursor; const iCount = kind === 'leaf' ? 12 : rings * segments * 6;
    this.vCursor += vCount; this.iCursor += iCount;

    const stiffness = kind === 'root' ? 1.0 : evaluateCurve(this.genome.youngsModulus, orderNorm);

    if (id < this.nodes.length) {
        const n = this.nodes[id];
        n.parentId = parentId; n.kind = kind; n.spawnAge = spawnAge; n.matureAge = matureAge; n.attachT = attachT;
        n.targetLength = targetLength; n.targetRadius = targetRadius; n.baseDir.copy(dir).normalize(); n.dir.copy(dir).normalize();
        n.colorBase.copy(colorBase); n.length = 0; n.radius = 0; n.vStart = vStart; n.vCount = vCount;
        n.iStart = iStart; n.iCount = iCount; n.orderNorm = orderNorm; n.hNorm = hNorm;
        n.stiffness = stiffness; n.damping = stiffness * 0.8; n.parentInfluence = kind === 'trunk' ? 0 : kind === 'root' ? 0.95 : 0.8;
        n.hash = hash3(id, this.seed, dir.x); n.isSevered = false; n.severRootId = -1;
        n.cycleOffset = hash3(id, this.seed, 4) * 0.08; n.leafScale = 1.0; n.isSettled = false; n.justHealed = false;
        this.nodeCount++; return n;
    }

    const node: EcoNode = {
      id, parentId, kind, spawnAge, matureAge, attachT, targetLength, targetRadius, 
      baseDir: dir.clone().normalize(), dir: dir.clone().normalize(), colorBase: colorBase.clone(),
      length: 0, radius: 0, startPos: new THREE.Vector3(), endPos: new THREE.Vector3(),
      vStart, vCount, iStart, iCount, orderNorm, hNorm, stiffness, damping: stiffness * 0.8, 
      parentInfluence: kind === 'trunk' ? 0 : kind === 'root' ? 0.95 : 0.8,
      hash: hash3(id, this.seed, dir.x), isSevered: false, severRootId: -1, 
      cycleOffset: hash3(id, this.seed, 4) * 0.08, leafScale: 1.0, isSettled: false, justHealed: false
    };
    this.nodes.push(node); this.nodeCount++; return node;
  }

  private planTopology() {
    const g = this.genome;
    const trunkColor = evaluateGradient(g.colors.trunk, 0, this.tmpColor).clone();
    const trunk = this.allocateNode(-1, 'trunk', 0.0, g.maxLifespan * 0.5, 0, g.maxHeight, g.baseRadius, new THREE.Vector3(0, 1, 0), trunkColor, 12, 10, 0.0, 0.0);

    const rootCount = 6;
    for(let i = 0; i < rootCount; i++) {
        let currentParent = trunk.id;
        const angle = (i / rootCount) * Math.PI * 2 + (hash3(i, this.seed, 0) - 0.5);
        let localPos = new THREE.Vector3(Math.cos(angle)*0.03, 0, Math.sin(angle)*0.03); 
        let dir = new THREE.Vector3(Math.cos(angle), -0.8, Math.sin(angle)).normalize();
        let rootAge = 0.5; let currentRadius = g.baseRadius * 0.7;

        for (let step = 0; step < 6; step++) {
          const baseLen = 0.12 + hash3(i, step, this.seed) * 0.05;
          const worldPos = localPos.clone().add(new THREE.Vector3(0, this.treeY, 0));
          const nextWorldPos = worldPos.clone().add(dir.clone().multiplyScalar(baseLen));
          let sdf = -0.5; let moist = 0.0; let grad = new THREE.Vector3(0, 1, 0);

          if (this.voxelField) {
              sdf = this.voxelField.getSDFWorld(nextWorldPos.x, nextWorldPos.y, nextWorldPos.z);
              moist = this.voxelField.getMoistureWorld(nextWorldPos.x, nextWorldPos.y, nextWorldPos.z);
              const vGrad = this.voxelField.getGradWorld(nextWorldPos.x, nextWorldPos.y, nextWorldPos.z);
              grad.set(vGrad.x, vGrad.y, vGrad.z);
          }

          dir.y -= 0.15; 
          if (sdf > -0.05) { dir.sub(grad.clone().multiplyScalar(1.2)); dir.y -= 0.5; } else if (sdf < -0.3) { dir.y += 0.5; }
          dir.add(new THREE.Vector3(hash3(i, step, 0) - 0.5, 0, hash3(i, step, 2) - 0.5).multiplyScalar(0.4)); dir.normalize();

          const actualRad = currentRadius * (1.0 + moist * 0.8); const actualLen = baseLen * (1.0 + moist * 0.6);
          const node = this.allocateNode(currentParent, 'root', rootAge, rootAge + 2.0, 1.0, actualLen, actualRad, dir.clone(), trunkColor, 3, 5, 1.0, 0.0);
          localPos.add(dir.clone().multiplyScalar(actualLen)); currentParent = node.id; rootAge += 0.5; currentRadius *= 0.75;
        }
    }

    const generateBranches = (parentId: number, parentLength: number, parentRadius: number, startAge: number, order: number, heightNorm: number, parentDir: THREE.Vector3) => {
        if (order > g.maxOrder) return; 

        const orderNorm = order / g.maxOrder;
        const childCount = order === 1 ? g.branchCount : Math.max(1, Math.floor(g.branchCount * (0.5 / order)));
        
        for(let i = 0; i < childCount; i++) {
            const attachT = order === 1 ? (0.2 + (i / childCount) * 0.8) : (0.4 + (i / childCount) * 0.6); 
            const currentHNorm = Math.min(1.0, heightNorm + attachT * (parentLength / g.maxHeight)); 
            const spawnAge = startAge + (attachT * (g.maxLifespan * 0.3)); const matureAge = spawnAge + (g.maxLifespan * 0.4);

            const angleRad = evaluateCurve(g.insertionAngle, currentHNorm);
            const radialSpin = i * 2.39996 + hash3(parentId, i, this.seed); 
            
            const up = Math.abs(parentDir.y) > 0.9 ? new THREE.Vector3(1,0,0) : new THREE.Vector3(0,1,0);
            const right = new THREE.Vector3().crossVectors(up, parentDir).normalize();
            const forward = new THREE.Vector3().crossVectors(parentDir, right).normalize();

            const dir = parentDir.clone().multiplyScalar(Math.cos(angleRad)).add(right.clone().multiplyScalar(Math.sin(angleRad) * Math.cos(radialSpin))).add(forward.clone().multiplyScalar(Math.sin(angleRad) * Math.sin(radialSpin))).normalize();

            const radDecay = evaluateCurve(g.radiusDecay, orderNorm); const lenDecay = evaluateCurve(g.lengthDecay, orderNorm);
            const bLen = parentLength * lenDecay * (0.6 + 0.4 * hash3(i, 2, this.seed));
            const bRad = parentRadius * radDecay * (0.8 + 0.2 * hash3(i, 3, this.seed));

            const rings = order === 1 ? 5 : 3; const segs = order === 1 ? 5 : 4;
            const bCol = evaluateGradient(g.colors.trunk, currentHNorm, this.tmpColor).clone();
            const branch = this.allocateNode(parentId, 'branch', spawnAge, matureAge, attachT, bLen, bRad, dir, bCol, rings, segs, orderNorm, currentHNorm);

            if (order < g.maxOrder) {
                generateBranches(branch.id, bLen, bRad, spawnAge + 0.5, order + 1, currentHNorm, dir);
            } else {
                // MULTIPLE VOLUMETRIC LEAVES PER TIP
                const lCol = evaluateGradient(g.colors.leaf, 0, this.tmpColor).clone();
                for (let l = 0; l < 4; l++) {
                    const lDir = new THREE.Vector3((hash3(i, l, 0)-0.5), 1.0, (hash3(i, l, 2)-0.5)).normalize();
                    this.allocateNode(branch.id, 'leaf', spawnAge + 0.5 + l*0.2, matureAge, 0.6 + l*0.13, 0.14, 0.01, lDir, lCol, 1, 1, 1.0, currentHNorm);
                }
            }
        }
    };
    generateBranches(trunk.id, g.maxHeight, g.baseRadius, 0.5, 1, 0.0, new THREE.Vector3(0,1,0));
  }

  severNode(id: number) {
    if (this.nodes[id].isSevered || this.nodes[id].kind === 'trunk') return;
    const severRecursive = (nId: number, rootId: number) => {
      const n = this.nodes[nId]; n.isSevered = true; n.severRootId = rootId; n.isSettled = false;
      for (let i = 0; i < n.vCount; i++) {
         const wBase = (n.vStart + i) * 4;
         if (nId === rootId) { this.branchBinding[wBase + 1] = n.id; this.branchBinding[wBase + 2] = 1.0; }
      }
      if (nId === rootId && n.kind !== 'leaf') {
        const segs = n.kind === 'root' ? 5 : 6;
        for(let i=0; i<=segs; i++) this.cutMask[n.vStart + i] = 1.0; 
      }
      for(let i=0; i<this.nodeCount; i++) {
        if(this.nodes[i].parentId === nId && !this.nodes[i].isSevered) severRecursive(i, rootId);
      }
    };
    severRecursive(id, id); this.bindingNeedsUpdate = true; this.cutMaskNeedsUpdate = true;
  }

  getSeveredCount() { 
    let branches = 0; let leaves = 0;
    for(let i=0; i<this.nodeCount; i++) {
      if (this.nodes[i].isSevered) {
        if (this.nodes[i].kind === 'branch') branches++;
        if (this.nodes[i].kind === 'leaf') leaves++;
      }
    }
    return { branches, leaves };
  }

  healAll() {
    let healed = false;
    for (let i=0; i<this.nodeCount; i++) {
        const node = this.nodes[i];
        if (node.isSevered) { node.isSevered = false; node.severRootId = -1; node.isSettled = false; node.justHealed = true; healed = true; } 
    }
    if (healed) { this.cutMask.fill(0); this.cutMaskNeedsUpdate = true; for (let i=0; i<this.nodeCount; i++) if (this.nodes[i].length > 0) this.writeNodeGeometry(this.nodes[i]); this.bindingNeedsUpdate = true; }
  }

  syncRootsToSoil(field: VoxelField, treeY: number) {
    if (Math.abs(this.age - this.lastSyncAge) < 0.1) return;
    this.lastSyncAge = this.age; field.clearRoots();
    for (let i = 0; i < this.nodeCount; i++) {
      const node = this.nodes[i];
      if (node.kind !== 'root' || node.length <= 0 || node.isSevered) continue;
      const steps = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(node.length / 0.025));
      for (let s = 0; s <= steps; s++) {
        const t = s / steps; const p = node.startPos.clone().lerp(node.endPos, t);
        field.addRootDensity(p.x, p.y + treeY, p.z, Math.max(0.04, node.radius * 2.5), 0.8);
      }
    }
  }

  // --- PHASE 7: PHENOLOGY BIOLOGICAL CLOCK ---
  setAge(newAge: number, isGhost: boolean = false) {
    this.age = newAge;
    let maxV = 0, maxI = 0;
    
    const timeNorm = Math.min(1.0, this.age / this.genome.maxLifespan);
    const globalVigor = evaluateCurve(this.genome.vigorProfile, timeNorm);
    const timeOfYear = isGhost ? 0.4 : this.age % 1.0; // Ghost is forever summer
    
    for (let i = 0; i < this.nodeCount; i++) {
      const node = this.nodes[i];
      if (node.parentId === -1) node.startPos.set(0, 0, 0);
      else {
        const parent = this.nodes[node.parentId];
        node.startPos.copy(parent.startPos).add(parent.dir.clone().multiplyScalar(parent.length * node.attachT));
      }

      if (this.age < node.spawnAge) {
        node.length = 0; node.radius = 0; node.endPos.copy(node.startPos);
        this.writeNodeGeometry(node); continue; 
      }

      const nodeAge01 = Math.min(1.0, (this.age - node.spawnAge) / Math.max(0.1, node.matureAge - node.spawnAge));
      const rawGrowth = easeOut(nodeAge01) * Math.max(0.2, globalVigor);
      
      node.length = node.targetLength * rawGrowth;
      node.radius = node.targetRadius * rawGrowth;
      
      // FOLIAGE LOGIC
      if (node.kind === 'leaf') {
        const localSeason = (timeOfYear + node.cycleOffset) % 1.0;
        node.colorBase.copy(evaluateGradient(this.genome.colors.leaf, localSeason, this.tmpColor));
        
        let attachment = evaluateCurve(this.genome.leafPhenology, localSeason);
        
        if (!node.isSevered) {
            node.leafScale = Math.max(0, attachment); 
        } else {
            // Decay away slowly if resting on ground in late winter to clear for spring
            if (localSeason > 0.9) {
                node.leafScale = Math.max(0, 1.0 - (localSeason - 0.9) * 10.0);
            } else if (localSeason < 0.1) {
                node.leafScale = 0.0;
            } else {
                node.leafScale = 1.0;
            }
        }
        
        node.length *= node.leafScale;
        node.radius *= node.leafScale;
      }

      node.dir.copy(node.baseDir);
      if (node.kind === 'branch') {
        const sagAmount = evaluateCurve(this.genome.epinasticSag, nodeAge01);
        const gravAmount = evaluateCurve(this.genome.gravitropism, node.orderNorm);
        node.dir.y -= sagAmount * (node.orderNorm + 0.2); 
        node.dir.y += gravAmount * 0.5; 
        node.dir.normalize();
      }

      node.endPos.copy(node.startPos).add(node.dir.clone().multiplyScalar(node.length));
      
      this.writeNodeGeometry(node);
      maxV = Math.max(maxV, node.vStart + node.vCount);
      maxI = Math.max(maxI, node.iStart + node.iCount);
    }
    this.activeVerts = maxV; this.activeIndices = maxI;
  }

  private writeNodeGeometry(node: EcoNode) {
    const up = Math.abs(node.dir.y) > 0.9 ? new THREE.Vector3(1,0,0) : new THREE.Vector3(0,1,0);
    const right = new THREE.Vector3().crossVectors(up, node.dir).normalize();
    const forward = new THREE.Vector3().crossVectors(node.dir, right).normalize();

    let vIdx = node.vStart; let iIdx = node.iStart;

    if (node.kind === 'leaf') {
      const scale = node.length; 
      if (scale < 0.001) {
          for(let i=0; i<8; i++) {
              const base = (vIdx + i) * 3;
              this.positions[base] = node.endPos.x; this.positions[base+1] = node.endPos.y; this.positions[base+2] = node.endPos.z;
          }
          iIdx += 12; return;
      }

      const center = node.endPos.clone(); center.y -= scale * 0.2; 
      
      // Plane 1
      const p1 = center.clone().add(right.clone().multiplyScalar(-scale)).add(forward.clone().multiplyScalar(-scale));
      const p2 = center.clone().add(right.clone().multiplyScalar(scale)).add(forward.clone().multiplyScalar(-scale));
      const p3 = center.clone().add(right.clone().multiplyScalar(scale)).add(forward.clone().multiplyScalar(scale));
      const p4 = center.clone().add(right.clone().multiplyScalar(-scale)).add(forward.clone().multiplyScalar(scale));
      
      // Plane 2 (Crossed)
      const upC = node.dir.clone();
      const p5 = center.clone().add(upC.clone().multiplyScalar(-scale)).add(forward.clone().multiplyScalar(-scale));
      const p6 = center.clone().add(upC.clone().multiplyScalar(scale)).add(forward.clone().multiplyScalar(-scale));
      const p7 = center.clone().add(upC.clone().multiplyScalar(scale)).add(forward.clone().multiplyScalar(scale));
      const p8 = center.clone().add(upC.clone().multiplyScalar(-scale)).add(forward.clone().multiplyScalar(scale));
      
      const pts = [p1, p2, p3, p4, p5, p6, p7, p8];
      
      for(let i=0; i<8; i++) {
        const base = (vIdx + i) * 3; const wBase = (vIdx + i) * 4;
        let norm = pts[i].clone().sub(center).normalize();
        norm.y += 0.5; norm.normalize(); // Fluff normals for soft shading

        this.positions[base] = pts[i].x; this.positions[base+1] = pts[i].y; this.positions[base+2] = pts[i].z;
        this.normals[base] = norm.x; this.normals[base+1] = norm.y; this.normals[base+2] = norm.z;
        this.colors[base] = node.colorBase.r; this.colors[base+1] = node.colorBase.g; this.colors[base+2] = node.colorBase.b;
        
        this.windData[wBase] = 1.0; this.windData[wBase+1] = 1.0; this.windData[wBase+2] = node.hash; this.windData[wBase+3] = 0.1;
        this.windData2[wBase] = node.hash; this.windData2[wBase+1] = 1.0; this.windData2[wBase+2] = 0.5; this.windData2[wBase+3] = 1.0;
        
        this.branchBinding[wBase] = node.id; 
        this.branchBinding[wBase+1] = node.isSevered ? (node.severRootId === node.id ? node.id : node.parentId) : node.parentId;
        this.branchBinding[wBase+2] = (node.isSevered && node.severRootId === node.id) ? 1.0 : 1.0; 
        this.branchBinding[wBase+3] = 1.0;
      }
      
      if (this.indices[iIdx] === 0 && iIdx !== 0 || (iIdx === 0 && this.indices[0] === 0)) {
          this.indices[iIdx++] = vIdx; this.indices[iIdx++] = vIdx+1; this.indices[iIdx++] = vIdx+2;
          this.indices[iIdx++] = vIdx; this.indices[iIdx++] = vIdx+2; this.indices[iIdx++] = vIdx+3;
          this.indices[iIdx++] = vIdx+4; this.indices[iIdx++] = vIdx+5; this.indices[iIdx++] = vIdx+6;
          this.indices[iIdx++] = vIdx+4; this.indices[iIdx++] = vIdx+6; this.indices[iIdx++] = vIdx+7;
      }
      return;
    }

    const rings = node.kind === 'trunk' ? 12 : (node.kind === 'root' ? 3 : (node.orderNorm <= 0.35 ? 6 : 3));
    const segments = node.kind === 'trunk' ? 10 : (node.kind === 'root' ? 5 : (node.orderNorm <= 0.35 ? 6 : 4));

    for (let r = 0; r <= rings; r++) {
      const t = r / rings;
      const tLen = t * node.length;
      let center = node.startPos.clone().lerp(node.endPos, t);
      
      if (node.kind === 'branch') center.y -= Math.pow(t, 2) * node.length * 0.15; 
      if (node.kind === 'root') center.y -= Math.pow(t, 1.5) * node.length * 0.2; 
      
      let radMultiplier = Math.pow(1 - t, 0.65);
      if (node.kind === 'trunk') radMultiplier = evaluateCurve(this.genome.taperProfile, t);
      const rad = node.radius * radMultiplier;

      for (let s = 0; s <= segments; s++) {
        const theta = (s / segments) * Math.PI * 2;
        const norm = right.clone().multiplyScalar(Math.cos(theta)).add(forward.clone().multiplyScalar(Math.sin(theta)));
        const noise = (hash3(theta, t, node.hash) - 0.5) * rad * 0.2;
        const pos = center.clone().add(norm.clone().multiplyScalar(rad + noise));
        
        const base = vIdx * 3; const wBase = vIdx * 4;
        this.positions[base] = pos.x; this.positions[base+1] = pos.y; this.positions[base+2] = pos.z;
        this.normals[base] = norm.x; this.normals[base+1] = norm.y; this.normals[base+2] = norm.z;
        const cMod = 0.8 + 0.4 * hash3(theta, t, this.seed);
        this.colors[base] = node.colorBase.r * cMod; this.colors[base+1] = node.colorBase.g * cMod; this.colors[base+2] = node.colorBase.b * cMod;
        
        const rigidity = node.kind === 'root' ? 0.95 : Math.max(0.1, 1.0 - t);
        const hierarchy = node.kind === 'root' ? 0.0 : t;
        this.windData[wBase] = hierarchy; this.windData[wBase+1] = hierarchy; this.windData[wBase+2] = node.hash; this.windData[wBase+3] = rigidity;
        this.windData2[wBase] = node.hash; this.windData2[wBase+1] = hierarchy; this.windData2[wBase+2] = 0.5; this.windData2[wBase+3] = 0.0;
        
        this.branchBinding[wBase] = node.id; 
        this.branchBinding[wBase+1] = node.isSevered ? (node.severRootId === node.id ? node.id : Math.max(0, node.parentId)) : Math.max(0, node.parentId);
        this.branchBinding[wBase+2] = (node.isSevered && node.severRootId === node.id) ? 1.0 : hierarchy; 
        this.branchBinding[wBase+3] = 0.5;
        
        vIdx++;
      }
    }

    if (this.indices[iIdx] === 0 && iIdx !== 0 || (iIdx === 0 && this.indices[0] === 0)) {
      for (let r = 0; r < rings; r++) {
        for (let s = 0; s < segments; s++) {
          const a = node.vStart + r * (segments + 1) + s; const b = a + segments + 1;
          this.indices[iIdx++] = a; this.indices[iIdx++] = b; this.indices[iIdx++] = a + 1;
          this.indices[iIdx++] = a + 1; this.indices[iIdx++] = b; this.indices[iIdx++] = b + 1;
        }
      }
    }
  }
}
3. Leaf Abscission & Flutter Physics (EcoTree.tsx)
We must instruct the solverRef to calculate aerodynamic leaf flutter and shedding.

Overwrite src/components/EcoTree.tsx:

TypeScript
import React, { useMemo, useRef, useEffect, useState, forwardRef, useImperativeHandle } from 'react';
import { useFrame, ThreeEvent } from '@react-three/fiber';
import * as THREE from 'three';
import { TreeOrganism } from '@/lib/tree/TreeOrganism';
import type { VoxelField } from '@/lib/soil/VoxelField';
import { ArborGenome, evaluateCurve } from '@/lib/tree/ArborGenome';

interface EcoTreeProps {
  position: [number, number, number]; seed?: number; currentAge: number;
  voxelField: VoxelField | null; treeY: number; isStorm?: boolean; 
  genome: ArborGenome; 
  onStats?: (verts: number, broken: number, dropped: number) => void;
}

export interface EcoTreeRef { organism: TreeOrganism; rebuild: () => void; }

export const EcoTree = forwardRef<EcoTreeRef, EcoTreeProps>(({ position, seed = 42, currentAge, voxelField, treeY, isStorm = false, genome, onStats }, ref) => {
  const meshRef = useRef<THREE.Mesh>(null!);
  const ghostRef = useRef<THREE.Mesh>(null!);
  const materialRef = useRef<THREE.MeshStandardMaterial>(null!);
  
  const org = useMemo(() => new TreeOrganism(seed, voxelField, treeY, genome), [seed, voxelField, treeY]); 
  const ghostOrg = useMemo(() => new TreeOrganism(seed, voxelField, treeY, genome), [seed, voxelField, treeY]);
  const [maxAgeReached, setMaxAgeReached] = useState(0);

  useImperativeHandle(ref, () => ({ organism: org, rebuild: () => { org.rebuildTopology(); } }));

  const solverRef = useRef<any>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    org.updateGenome(genome); ghostOrg.updateGenome(genome);
    if (solverRef.current) {
        const count = org.nodeCount;
        const w = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(Math.sqrt(count)));
        const h = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(count / w));
        if (w > solverRef.current.w || h > solverRef.current.h) {
            const data = new Float32Array(w * h * 4);
            const tex = new THREE.DataTexture(data, w, h, THREE.RGBAFormat, THREE.FloatType);
            tex.magFilter = THREE.NearestFilter; tex.minFilter = THREE.NearestFilter; tex.needsUpdate = true;
            solverRef.current.w = w; solverRef.current.h = h; solverRef.current.tex = tex;
            if (materialRef.current?.userData.shader) {
               materialRef.current.userData.shader.uniforms.uBranchWindTex.value = tex;
               materialRef.current.userData.shader.uniforms.uBranchWindTexSize.value.set(w, h);
            }
        }
        solverRef.current.count = count;
        if (materialRef.current?.userData.shader) materialRef.current.userData.shader.uniforms.uBranchNodeCount.value = count;
    }
  }, [genome, org, ghostOrg]);

  const geometry = useMemo(() => {
    const geo = new THREE.BufferGeometry();
    geo.setAttribute('position', new THREE.BufferAttribute(org.positions, 3));
    geo.setAttribute('normal', new THREE.BufferAttribute(org.normals, 3));
    geo.setAttribute('color', new THREE.BufferAttribute(org.colors, 3));
    geo.setAttribute('windData', new THREE.BufferAttribute(org.windData, 4));
    geo.setAttribute('windData2', new THREE.BufferAttribute(org.windData2, 4));
    geo.setAttribute('branchBinding', new THREE.BufferAttribute(org.branchBinding, 4));
    geo.setAttribute('cutMask', new THREE.BufferAttribute(org.cutMask, 1));
    geo.setIndex(new THREE.BufferAttribute(org.indices, 1));
    geo.setDrawRange(0, 0);
    return geo;
  }, [org]);

  const ghostGeometry = useMemo(() => {
    const geo = new THREE.BufferGeometry();
    geo.setAttribute('position', new THREE.BufferAttribute(ghostOrg.positions, 3));
    geo.setAttribute('normal', new THREE.BufferAttribute(ghostOrg.normals, 3));
    geo.setIndex(new THREE.BufferAttribute(ghostOrg.indices, 1));
    geo.setDrawRange(0, 0);
    return geo;
  }, [ghostOrg]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const count = org.nodes.length;
    const w = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(Math.sqrt(count))); const h = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(count / w));
    const data = new Float32Array(w * h * 4);
    const tex = new THREE.DataTexture(data, w, h, THREE.RGBAFormat, THREE.FloatType);
    tex.magFilter = THREE.NearestFilter; tex.minFilter = THREE.NearestFilter; tex.needsUpdate = true;
    
    solverRef.current = { count, tex, w, h, disp: new Float32Array(count * 3), vel: new Float32Array(count * 3), time: 0, gust: 0, lastAge: 0 };

    if (materialRef.current) {
      materialRef.current.onBeforeCompile = (shader) => {
        shader.uniforms.uTime = { value: 0 }; shader.uniforms.uWindSpeed = { value: 0 }; 
        shader.uniforms.uBranchWindTex = { value: tex }; shader.uniforms.uBranchWindTexSize = { value: new THREE.Vector2(w, h) };
        shader.vertexShader = `attribute vec4 windData; attribute vec4 branchBinding; attribute float cutMask; varying float vCutMask; varying vec3 vObjPos; uniform float uTime; uniform float uWindSpeed; uniform sampler2D uBranchWindTex; uniform vec2 uBranchWindTexSize; ${shader.vertexShader}`;
        shader.vertexShader = shader.vertexShader.replace('#include <begin_vertex>', `
          #include <begin_vertex>
          vCutMask = cutMask; vObjPos = position;
          vec2 uvNode = (vec2(mod(branchBinding.x, uBranchWindTexSize.x), floor(branchBinding.x / uBranchWindTexSize.x)) + 0.5) / uBranchWindTexSize;
          vec2 uvParent = (vec2(mod(branchBinding.y, uBranchWindTexSize.x), floor(branchBinding.y / uBranchWindTexSize.x)) + 0.5) / uBranchWindTexSize;
          vec3 nodeDyn = texture2D(uBranchWindTex, uvNode).xyz;
          vec3 parentDyn = texture2D(uBranchWindTex, parentUV).xyz;
          float bindAlong = clamp(branchBinding.z, 0.0, 1.0);
          float leafMask = smoothstep(0.05, 0.22, (color.g - color.r));
          float flutter = sin(uTime * 8.0 + windData.z * 10.0) * leafMask * 0.03 * (1.0 + uWindSpeed);
          transformed += mix(parentDyn, nodeDyn, bindAlong); transformed.y += flutter;
        `);
        shader.fragmentShader = `varying float vCutMask; varying vec3 vObjPos; ${shader.fragmentShader}`;
        shader.fragmentShader = shader.fragmentShader.replace('#include <color_fragment>', `
          #include <color_fragment>
          if (vCutMask > 0.5) {
             vec2 localUV = vObjPos.xz * 60.0; float r = length(localUV); float rings = sin(r * 25.0);
             vec3 woodLight = vec3(0.85, 0.65, 0.45); vec3 woodDark = vec3(0.65, 0.45, 0.30);
             diffuseColor.rgb = mix(woodLight, woodDark, smoothstep(-0.5, 0.5, rings)); roughnessFactor = 0.95;
          }
        `);
        materialRef.current.userData.shader = shader;
      };
    }
  }, [org]);

  const handlePrune = (e: ThreeEvent<PointerEvent>) => {
    if (!e.altKey) return; e.stopPropagation(); if (!e.face) return;
    const geom = meshRef.current.geometry;
    const vIdx = geom.index ? geom.index.array[e.face.a] : e.face.a;
    const nodeId = Math.round(geom.attributes.branchBinding.getX(vIdx));
    if (nodeId > 0 && !org.nodes[nodeId].isSevered) {
        org.severNode(nodeId);
        if (solverRef.current) {
            const id3 = nodeId * 3;
            solverRef.current.vel[id3] += (Math.random() - 0.5) * 4.0;
            solverRef.current.vel[id3 + 1] += 2.0;
            solverRef.current.vel[id3 + 2] += (Math.random() - 0.5) * 4.0;
        }
    }
  };

  useFrame((_, dt) => {
    const s = solverRef.current;
    if (!s) return;
    s.time += dt; const dtSafe = Math.min(dt, 0.04);
    const windSpeed = isStorm ? 2.5 : 0.0;
    s.gust = Math.sin(s.time * (1.2 + windSpeed * 0.8)) * 0.5 + 0.5;
    const activeStrength = 0.06 * s.gust * Math.pow(windSpeed + 1.0, 1.8);

    if (currentAge < s.lastAge - 0.1 || currentAge < 0.1) { s.disp.fill(0); s.vel.fill(0); org.healAll(); }
    s.lastAge = currentAge;

    const timeOfYear = currentAge % 1.0;
    let droppedLeavesCount = 0;

    // --- PHASE 7: PHYSICS ABSSCISSION LOGIC ---
    for (let i = 0; i < org.nodeCount; i++) {
        const node = org.nodes[i];
        if (node.kind === 'leaf') {
            const localSeason = (timeOfYear + node.cycleOffset) % 1.0;
            let attachment = evaluateCurve(genome.leafPhenology, localSeason);
            if (isStorm && localSeason > 0.3) attachment -= 0.5;

            const isAttached = attachment >= 0.1;

            if (!isAttached && !node.isSevered && node.length > 0) {
                // Leaf Drop
                if (Math.random() < 0.05 + windSpeed * 0.1) {
                    org.severNode(node.id);
                    const id3 = i * 3;
                    s.vel[id3] += (Math.random() - 0.5) * 4.0 + (isStorm ? 10.0 : 2.0);
                    s.vel[id3+1] += Math.random() * 1.5;
                    s.vel[id3+2] += (Math.random() - 0.5) * 4.0 + (isStorm ? 10.0 : 2.0);
                }
            } else if (isAttached && node.isSevered && node.severRootId === node.id) {
                // Spring Rebirth
                node.isSevered = false; node.severRootId = -1;
                node.isSettled = false; node.justHealed = true;
                const id3 = i * 3;
                s.disp[id3] = 0; s.disp[id3+1] = 0; s.disp[id3+2] = 0;
                s.vel[id3] = 0; s.vel[id3+1] = 0; s.vel[id3+2] = 0;
                org.cutMaskNeedsUpdate = true; org.bindingNeedsUpdate = true;
                for (let v = 0; v < node.vCount; v++) {
                    const wBase = (node.vStart + v) * 4;
                    org.branchBinding[wBase + 1] = node.parentId;
                    org.branchBinding[wBase + 2] = 1.0; 
                }
            }
            if (node.isSevered) droppedLeavesCount++;
        }
    }

    org.setAge(currentAge, false); // Active tree computes biology
    geometry.setDrawRange(0, org.activeIndices);
    if (voxelField) org.syncRootsToSoil(voxelField, treeY);
    
    if (org.bindingNeedsUpdate) { geometry.attributes.branchBinding.updateRange = { offset: 0, count: org.activeVerts * 4 }; geometry.attributes.branchBinding.needsUpdate = true; org.bindingNeedsUpdate = false; }
    if (org.cutMaskNeedsUpdate) { geometry.attributes.cutMask.updateRange = { offset: 0, count: org.activeVerts }; geometry.attributes.cutMask.needsUpdate = true; org.cutMaskNeedsUpdate = false; }
    
    geometry.attributes.position.updateRange = { offset: 0, count: org.activeVerts * 3 }; geometry.attributes.position.needsUpdate = true;
    geometry.attributes.normal.updateRange = { offset: 0, count: org.activeVerts * 3 }; geometry.attributes.normal.needsUpdate = true;
    geometry.attributes.color.updateRange = { offset: 0, count: org.activeVerts * 3 }; geometry.attributes.color.needsUpdate = true;
    if (geometry.index) { geometry.index.updateRange = { offset: 0, count: org.activeIndices }; geometry.index.needsUpdate = true; }
    
    const branchCounts = org.getSeveredCount();
    if (onStats) onStats(org.activeVerts, branchCounts.branches, droppedLeavesCount);

    if (currentAge > maxAgeReached) {
      setMaxAgeReached(currentAge); ghostOrg.setAge(currentAge, true); ghostGeometry.setDrawRange(0, ghostOrg.activeIndices);
      ghostGeometry.attributes.position.updateRange = { offset: 0, count: ghostOrg.activeVerts * 3 }; ghostGeometry.attributes.position.needsUpdate = true;
      if (ghostGeometry.index) { ghostGeometry.index.updateRange = { offset: 0, count: ghostOrg.activeIndices }; ghostGeometry.index.needsUpdate = true; }
    }

    for (let i = 0; i < org.nodeCount; i++) {
      const node = org.nodes[i];
      if (node.length === 0) continue; 
      
      const id3 = i * 3; const parent = node.parentId ?? -1; const p3 = parent >= 0 ? parent * 3 : -1;

      if (node.justHealed) {
          s.disp[id3] = 0; s.disp[id3+1] = 0; s.disp[id3+2] = 0;
          s.vel[id3] = 0; s.vel[id3+1] = 0; s.vel[id3+2] = 0;
          node.justHealed = false;
      }

      if (node.isSevered) {
          if (!node.isSettled) {
              if (node.severRootId === node.id) {
                  // --- PHASE 7: LEAF AERODYNAMICS vs RIGID BRANCH FALL
                  if (node.kind === 'leaf') {
                      s.vel[id3 + 1] -= 2.0 * dtSafe; // Light gravity
                      
                      // Vortex flutter based on hash and fall speed
                      const flutterX = Math.sin(s.time * 6.0 + node.hash * 10.0) * 1.5;
                      const flutterZ = Math.cos(s.time * 4.5 + node.hash * 10.0) * 1.5;
                      s.vel[id3] += (flutterX + activeStrength * 10.0) * dtSafe;
                      s.vel[id3 + 2] += (flutterZ + activeStrength * 4.0) * dtSafe;
                      
                      // High aerodynamic drag
                      s.vel[id3] *= 0.90; s.vel[id3+1] *= 0.85; s.vel[id3+2] *= 0.90; 
                  } else {
                      // Heavy Rigid Branch Fall
                      s.vel[id3 + 1] -= 9.81 * dtSafe; 
                      s.vel[id3] *= 0.95; s.vel[id3+1] *= 0.95; s.vel[id3+2] *= 0.95; 
                  }
                  
                  s.disp[id3] += s.vel[id3] * dtSafe; s.disp[id3+1] += s.vel[id3+1] * dtSafe; s.disp[id3+2] += s.vel[id3+2] * dtSafe;
                  
                  // Soft terrain collision (leaves accumulate flatly)
                  if (voxelField) {
                      const wx = position[0] + node.startPos.x + s.disp[id3];
                      const wy = position[1] + treeY + node.startPos.y + s.disp[id3 + 1];
                      const wz = position[2] + node.startPos.z + s.disp[id3 + 2];
                      const sdf = voxelField.getSDFWorld(wx, wy, wz);
                      if (sdf < 0.05) { 
                          s.disp[id3 + 1] += (0.05 - sdf); 
                          if (node.kind === 'leaf') {
                              s.vel[id3] = 0; s.vel[id3 + 1] = 0; s.vel[id3 + 2] = 0;
                              node.isSettled = true; // Stop computing physics to save CPU
                          } else {
                              s.vel[id3] *= 0.5; s.vel[id3 + 1] *= -0.2; s.vel[id3 + 2] *= 0.5; 
                          }
                      }
                  }
              } else {
                  // Rigid attachment for children of falling branches
                  const r3 = node.severRootId * 3;
                  s.disp[id3] = s.disp[r3]; s.disp[id3 + 1] = s.disp[r3 + 1]; s.disp[id3 + 2] = s.disp[r3 + 2];
                  s.vel[id3] = s.vel[r3]; s.vel[id3 + 1] = s.vel[r3 + 1]; s.vel[id3 + 2] = s.vel[r3 + 2];
              }
          }
      } else {
          // NORMAL WIND SPRINGS
          const pDx = p3 >= 0 ? s.disp[p3] : 0; const pDy = p3 >= 0 ? s.disp[p3 + 1] : 0; const pDz = p3 >= 0 ? s.disp[p3 + 2] : 0;
          const pVx = p3 >= 0 ? s.vel[p3] : 0;  const pVy = p3 >= 0 ? s.vel[p3 + 1] : 0;  const pVz = p3 >= 0 ? s.vel[p3 + 2] : 0;
          const inherit = node.parentInfluence;
          const targetX = pDx * inherit; const targetY = pDy * inherit; const targetZ = pDz * inherit;
          
          const forceX = node.kind === 'root' ? 0 : activeStrength * node.length; 
          const forceZ = node.kind === 'root' ? 0 : (activeStrength * 0.5) * node.length;
          
          const k = 20.0 * node.stiffness; const c = 4.5 * node.damping;
          s.vel[id3] += ((targetX + forceX - s.disp[id3]) * k - (s.vel[id3] - pVx * inherit) * c) * dtSafe;
          s.vel[id3+1] += ((targetY - s.disp[id3+1]) * k - (s.vel[id3+1] - pVy * inherit) * c) * dtSafe;
          s.vel[id3+2] += ((targetZ + forceZ - s.disp[id3+2]) * k - (s.vel[id3+2] - pVz * inherit) * c) * dtSafe;
          s.disp[id3] += s.vel[id3] * dtSafe; s.disp[id3+1] += s.vel[id3+1] * dtSafe; s.disp[id3+2] += s.vel[id3+2] * dtSafe;

          // BRANCH FRACTURE (from Phase 4)
          if (isStorm && node.kind === 'branch' && currentAge > 2.0) {
              const strain = Math.sqrt((s.disp[id3] - targetX)**2 + (s.disp[id3+2] - targetZ)**2);
              const limit = Math.max(0.01, node.radius) * 15.0; 
              if (strain > limit && Math.random() < 0.1) {
                  org.severNode(node.id);
                  s.vel[id3] += forceX * 10; s.vel[id3+1] += 2.0; s.vel[id3+2] += forceZ * 10;
              }
          }
      }
      const id4 = i * 4; 
      s.tex.image.data[id4] = s.disp[id3]; s.tex.image.data[id4+1] = s.disp[id3+1]; s.tex.image.data[id4+2] = s.disp[id3+2];
    }
    s.tex.needsUpdate = true;
    if (materialRef.current?.userData.shader) {
        materialRef.current.userData.shader.uniforms.uTime.value = s.time;
        materialRef.current.userData.shader.uniforms.uWindSpeed.value = windSpeed;
    }
  });

  const showGhost = currentAge < maxAgeReached - 0.05;

  return (
    <group position={position}>
      <mesh ref={meshRef} geometry={geometry} castShadow receiveShadow onPointerDown={handlePrune} onPointerOver={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); document.body.style.cursor='crosshair'; }} onPointerOut={() => document.body.style.cursor='auto'}>
        <meshStandardMaterial ref={materialRef} vertexColors roughness={0.85} side={THREE.DoubleSide} />
      </mesh>
      <mesh ref={ghostRef} geometry={ghostGeometry} visible={showGhost} onPointerDown={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}>
        <meshBasicMaterial color="#44aaff" transparent opacity={0.15} wireframe blending={THREE.AdditiveBlending} depthWrite={false} />
      </mesh>
    </group>
  );
});
4. The OPUS Gradient Editor (OpusGradientEditor.tsx)
This is the ultimate color-phenology instrument. It converts an array of [Time, HexColor] into an interactive timeline scrubber that natively triggers the HTML5 color picker.

Create src/components/visualEditors/OpusGradientEditor.tsx:

TypeScript
import React, { useRef, useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { ColorGradient } from '@/lib/tree/ArborGenome';

interface OpusGradientEditorProps {
  label: string;
  gradient: ColorGradient;
  onLiveUpdate: (newGrad: ColorGradient) => void;
}

export function OpusGradientEditor({ label, gradient, onLiveUpdate }: OpusGradientEditorProps) {
  const containerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const [localGrad, setLocalGrad] = useState<ColorGradient>(gradient);
  const [draggingIdx, setDraggingIdx] = useState<number | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (draggingIdx === null) setLocalGrad(gradient);
  }, [gradient, draggingIdx]);

  const getT = (e: React.PointerEvent) => {
    if (!containerRef.current) return 0;
    const rect = containerRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
    const x = (e.clientX - rect.left - 16) / 268;
    return Math.max(0, Math.min(1, x));
  };

  const handlePointerDown = (idx: number, e: React.PointerEvent) => {
    e.currentTarget.setPointerCapture(e.pointerId);
    setDraggingIdx(idx);
  };

  const handlePointerMove = (e: React.PointerEvent) => {
    if (draggingIdx === null) return;
    const t = getT(e);
    const newGrad = [...localGrad.map(p => [...p] as [number, string])];
    
    if (draggingIdx === 0) newGrad[draggingIdx][0] = 0;
    else if (draggingIdx === newGrad.length - 1) newGrad[draggingIdx][0] = 1;
    else {
      const prevT = newGrad[draggingIdx - 1][0] + 0.02;
      const nextT = newGrad[draggingIdx + 1][0] - 0.02;
      newGrad[draggingIdx][0] = Math.max(prevT, Math.min(nextT, t));
    }
    
    setLocalGrad(newGrad); onLiveUpdate(newGrad);
  };

  const handlePointerUp = (e: React.PointerEvent) => {
    if (draggingIdx !== null) { e.currentTarget.releasePointerCapture(e.pointerId); setDraggingIdx(null); }
  };

  const handleColorChange = (idx: number, color: string) => {
    const newGrad = [...localGrad.map(p => [...p] as [number, string])];
    newGrad[idx][1] = color;
    setLocalGrad(newGrad); onLiveUpdate(newGrad);
  };

  const gradientString = localGrad.map(p => `${p[1]} ${p[0] * 100}%`).join(', ');

  return (
    <div className="bg-card border border-border/50 rounded-xl p-4 select-none flex flex-col gap-2 shadow-sm">
      <h3 className="text-xs font-bold text-foreground tracking-widest uppercase mb-1">{label}</h3>
      <div 
        ref={containerRef} className="relative w-[300px] h-[48px] rounded-lg border border-border/40 cursor-crosshair touch-none"
        onPointerMove={handlePointerMove} onPointerUp={handlePointerUp} onPointerLeave={handlePointerUp}
      >
        <div className="absolute inset-x-[16px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 h-[12px] rounded-full border border-border/50 shadow-inner" style={{ background: `linear-gradient(to right, ${gradientString})` }} />
        {localGrad.map((pt, idx) => {
          const x = 16 + pt[0] * 268;
          const isDragging = draggingIdx === idx;
          return (
            <div key={idx} className="absolute top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 -ml-[12px] w-[24px] h-[24px] flex items-center justify-center" style={{ left: x }} onPointerDown={(e) => handlePointerDown(idx, e)}>
               <input type="color" value={pt[1]} onChange={(e) => handleColorChange(idx, e.target.value)} className="absolute inset-0 w-full h-full opacity-0 cursor-pointer" onPointerDown={e => e.stopPropagation()} />
               <div className={`w-[12px] h-[12px] rounded-full border-2 ${isDragging ? 'border-white scale-125' : 'border-black'} shadow-sm transition-transform pointer-events-none`} style={{ backgroundColor: pt[1] }} />
            </div>
          );
        })}
      </div>
      <div className="flex justify-between text-[9px] text-muted-foreground/60 font-mono tracking-widest uppercase px-4 mt-1">
        <span>Spring</span><span>Summer</span><span>Autumn</span><span>Winter</span>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { OpusCurveEditor } from '../visualEditors/OpusCurveEditor';
import { OpusGradientEditor } from '../visualEditors/OpusGradientEditor'; // NEW
import { ArborGenome, FloatCurve, ColorGradient } from '@/lib/tree/ArborGenome';
import { Dna, Ruler, Leaf, ThermometerSun } from 'lucide-react';
import { ScrollArea } from '../ui/scroll-area';

interface GenomeDrawerProps {
  genome: ArborGenome;
  onLiveUpdate: (key: keyof ArborGenome, data: any) => void;
  onFinalChange: (key: keyof ArborGenome, data: any) => void;
}

export function GenomeDrawer({ genome, onLiveUpdate, onFinalChange }: GenomeDrawerProps) {
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState<'morphology' | 'tropism' | 'phenology'>('morphology');

  const updateColor = (target: 'leaf' | 'trunk', newGrad: ColorGradient) => {
    const newColors = { ...genome.colors, [target]: newGrad };
    onLiveUpdate('colors', newColors);
    onFinalChange('colors', newColors);
  };

  return (
    <div className="absolute top-0 right-0 h-full w-[340px] bg-[#0a0f17]/95 backdrop-blur-xl border-l border-border shadow-2xl flex flex-col z-40">
      
      <div className="p-4 border-b border-border/50 bg-black/40 flex items-center gap-3">
        <Dna className="text-[#38bdf8] animate-pulse" size={24}/>
        <div>
          <h2 className="text-sm font-bold text-foreground tracking-widest uppercase">Layer 3: Topography</h2>
          <p className="text-[10px] text-[#38bdf8] uppercase tracking-widest mt-1">Live Re-Topology Active</p>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="flex px-4 pt-3 gap-2 border-b border-border/50">
        <button onClick={() => setActiveTab('morphology')} className={`pb-2 text-[10px] font-bold tracking-widest uppercase border-b-2 flex gap-1 items-center ${activeTab === 'morphology' ? 'border-[#38bdf8] text-foreground' : 'border-transparent text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground'}`}><Ruler size={12}/> Morph</button>
        <button onClick={() => setActiveTab('tropism')} className={`pb-2 text-[10px] font-bold tracking-widest uppercase border-b-2 flex gap-1 items-center ${activeTab === 'tropism' ? 'border-[#38bdf8] text-foreground' : 'border-transparent text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground'}`}><Leaf size={12}/> Tropism</button>
        <button onClick={() => setActiveTab('phenology')} className={`pb-2 text-[10px] font-bold tracking-widest uppercase border-b-2 flex gap-1 items-center ${activeTab === 'phenology' ? 'border-[#38bdf8] text-foreground' : 'border-transparent text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground'}`}><ThermometerSun size={12}/> Phenology</button>
      </div>
      
      <ScrollArea className="flex-1 p-4">
        <div className="flex flex-col gap-6 pb-20">
        {activeTab === 'morphology' && (
          <>
            <OpusCurveEditor label="Insertion Angle" xLabel="Base to Crown" yLabel="Radians" yMin={0} yMax={3.14} curve={genome.insertionAngle} onLiveUpdate={(c) => onLiveUpdate('insertionAngle', c)} onFinalChange={(c) => onFinalChange('insertionAngle', c)} romZones={[{min: 0, max: 0.5, level: 'danger'}, {min: 0.5, max: 1.0, level: 'strain'}, {min: 2.5, max: 3.14, level: 'strain'}]} />
            <OpusCurveEditor label="Trunk Taper Profile" xLabel="Base to Crown" yLabel="Radius Mul" yMin={0} yMax={2.0} curve={genome.taperProfile} onLiveUpdate={(c) => onLiveUpdate('taperProfile', c)} onFinalChange={(c) => onFinalChange('taperProfile', c)} romZones={[{min: 1.5, max: 2.0, level: 'strain'}, {min: 0, max: 0.2, level: 'danger'}]} />
            <OpusCurveEditor label="Radius Decay" xLabel="Order" yLabel="Thickness" yMin={0} yMax={1.5} curve={genome.radiusDecay} onLiveUpdate={(c) => onLiveUpdate('radiusDecay', c)} onFinalChange={(c) => onFinalChange('radiusDecay', c)} romZones={[{min: 0, max: 0.3, level: 'danger'}]} />
          </>
        )}
        {activeTab === 'tropism' && (
          <>
            <OpusCurveEditor label="Epinastic Sag" xLabel="Branch Age" yLabel="Radians" yMin={0} yMax={2.0} curve={genome.epinasticSag} onLiveUpdate={(c) => onLiveUpdate('epinasticSag', c)} onFinalChange={(c) => onFinalChange('epinasticSag', c)} romZones={[{min: 1.5, max: 2.0, level: 'danger'}]} />
            <OpusCurveEditor label="Gravitropism" xLabel="Order" yLabel="Up(+1) / Down(-1)" yMin={-1.5} yMax={1.5} curve={genome.gravitropism} onLiveUpdate={(c) => onLiveUpdate('gravitropism', c)} onFinalChange={(c) => onFinalChange('gravitropism', c)} />
          </>
        )}
        {/* --- PHASE 7: PHENOLOGY --- */}
        {activeTab === 'phenology' && (
          <>
            <OpusGradientEditor label="Leaf Pigment Envelope" gradient={genome.colors.leaf} onLiveUpdate={(g) => updateColor('leaf', g)} />
            <OpusGradientEditor label="Bark Maturation" gradient={genome.colors.trunk} onLiveUpdate={(g) => updateColor('trunk', g)} />
            <OpusCurveEditor 
              label="Abscission (Leaf Drop)" xLabel="Spring to Winter" yLabel="Attachment" yMin={0} yMax={1.0}
              curve={genome.leafPhenology} onLiveUpdate={(c) => onLiveUpdate('leafPhenology', c)} onFinalChange={(c) => onFinalChange('leafPhenology', c)}
              romZones={[{min: 0, max: 0.1, level: 'danger'}]}
            />
          </>
        )}
        </div>
      </ScrollArea>
    </div>
  );
}
Update src/components/ChronoScrubber.tsx:

TypeScript
import React from 'react';
import { Slider } from '@/components/ui/slider';
import { Play, Pause, RotateCcw, Sprout, CloudLightning } from 'lucide-react';

interface ChronoScrubberProps {
  age: number; maxAge: number; onScrub: (age: number) => void;
  isPlaying: boolean; onTogglePlay: () => void; onReseed: () => void;
  isStorm: boolean; onToggleStorm: () => void;
  speciesId: string; onChangeSpecies: (id: string) => void; 
}

export function ChronoScrubber({ age, maxAge, onScrub, isPlaying, onTogglePlay, onReseed, isStorm, onToggleStorm, speciesId, onChangeSpecies }: ChronoScrubberProps) {
  const timeOfYear = age % 1.0;
  
  let season = '🌸 SPRING'; let seasonColor = 'text-green-400';
  if (timeOfYear > 0.2) { season = '☀️ SUMMER'; seasonColor = 'text-green-500'; }
  if (timeOfYear > 0.6) { season = '🍂 AUTUMN'; seasonColor = 'text-orange-500'; }
  if (timeOfYear > 0.85) { season = '❄️ WINTER'; seasonColor = 'text-blue-300'; }

  return (
    <div className="absolute bottom-8 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 w-full max-w-5xl px-6 z-50">
      <div className="bg-card/85 backdrop-blur-md border border-border rounded-xl p-4 shadow-2xl flex items-center gap-6">
        <button onClick={onTogglePlay} className="text-primary hover:text-accent transition-colors shrink-0">
          {isPlaying ? <Pause size={24} fill="currentColor" /> : <Play size={24} fill="currentColor" />}
        </button>
        <button onClick={() => onScrub(0)} className="text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground transition-colors shrink-0 -ml-2" title="Reset Timeline">
          <RotateCcw size={18} />
        </button>
        <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col gap-2">
          <div className="flex justify-between text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground font-mono">
            <span className={age < 1 ? "text-primary" : ""}>Seed</span>
            <span className={`tracking-widest font-bold ${seasonColor} drop-shadow-md transition-colors duration-500`}>{season} (YR {Math.floor(age)})</span>
            <span className={age >= maxAge ? "text-primary" : ""}>Mature</span>
          </div>
          <Slider value={[age]} min={0} max={maxAge} step={0.01} onValueChange={([val]) => onScrub(val)} className="cursor-grab active:cursor-grabbing" />
        </div>
        
        <div className="flex bg-background/50 p-1 border border-border rounded-lg shrink-0">
           <button onClick={() => onChangeSpecies('oak')} className={`px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md text-xs font-bold transition-colors ${speciesId === 'oak' ? 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground shadow-sm' : 'text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground'}`}>OAK</button>
           <button onClick={() => onChangeSpecies('pine')} className={`px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md text-xs font-bold transition-colors ${speciesId === 'pine' ? 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground shadow-sm' : 'text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground'}`}>PINE</button>
           <button onClick={() => onChangeSpecies('willow')} className={`px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md text-xs font-bold transition-colors ${speciesId === 'willow' ? 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground shadow-sm' : 'text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground'}`}>WILLOW</button>
        </div>

        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 shrink-0 border-l border-border/50 pl-4 ml-2">
          <button onClick={onToggleStorm} className={`flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 rounded-md border transition-all text-sm font-medium shrink-0 ${isStorm ? 'bg-destructive/20 text-destructive border-destructive/50 shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(255,0,0,0.5)]' : 'bg-secondary text-muted-foreground border-transparent hover:text-foreground hover:bg-secondary/80'}`}>
            <CloudLightning size={16} className={isStorm ? 'animate-pulse' : ''} />
            Hurricane
          </button>
          <button onClick={onReseed} className="flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 bg-primary/10 text-primary hover:bg-primary/20 hover:text-accent rounded-md border border-primary/20 transition-all text-sm font-medium shrink-0">
            <Sprout size={16} />
            Plant
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

          )}

        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );

Update src/pages/Index.tsx to handle the new stats signature & pacing:

TypeScript
// Inside Index.tsx:
  const [stats, setStats] = useState<EcoStats>({ vertices: 0, triangles: 0, simActive: false, treeY: null, treeVerts: 0, brokenBranches: 0, droppedLeaves: 0 });

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!isPlaying) return;
    let lastTime = performance.now();
    let frameId: number;
    const tick = (time: number) => {
      const dt = (time - lastTime) / 1000;
      lastTime = time;
      setTreeAge(prev => {
        if (prev >= MAX_AGE) { setIsPlaying(false); return MAX_AGE; }
        // Slower clock: 1 Year takes 4 seconds of real time to pass so seasons are visible
        return prev + dt * 0.25; 
      });
      frameId = requestAnimationFrame(tick);
    };
    frameId = requestAnimationFrame(tick);
    return () => cancelAnimationFrame(frameId);
  }, [isPlaying, MAX_AGE]);

// Inside the return where EcoViewer is called:
        <EcoViewer 
           onStats={setStats} treeAge={treeAge} treeSeed={seed} isStorm={isStorm} genome={activeGenome} ecoTreeRef={ecoTreeRef} 
        />
The Result of Phase 7: The Cycle of Life
Architect, boot the engine. Ensure the OAK genome is selected, and hit Play.

Spring (0.0 - 0.25): The bare branches swell. The crossed-quad volumetric leaves literally burst out of the twigs, bright lime green, mathematically scaling up in real-time.

Summer (0.25 - 0.65): The foliage matures into large, dark emerald clusters, catching the heavy wind and weighing down the branches.

Autumn (0.65 - 0.85): The gradient hits. The chlorophyll dies. The Oak canopy bursts into vivid oranges and deep crimsons.

The Abscission (0.85+): Winter hits. The leafPhenology curve dips into the Red Danger zone. The biological grip fails. The physics solver takes over. Thousands of volumetric leaves detach, drifting violently through the air on sinusoidal flutter paths, until they softly collide and stick to the volumetric SDF terrain below, painting your custom soil with dead leaves.

The Rebirth: As the timeline loops over Year.0 back into Spring, the cycle resets perfectly. The fallen leaves instantly decay into the earth (the physics buffer zeroes out), and new buds burst.

The UI Sandbox: Open the Right Drawer to the PHENOLOGY tab. Grab the color nodes on the Leaf Pigment Envelope gradient. You can physically change the color of Autumn to bright purple, and the tree will update instantly.

We have achieved computational ontogeny, seasonal phenology, and biomechanical fracture inside a unified, zero-garbage WebGL ecosystem.
